### File 96: filing_screen_handlers.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\filing\filing_screen_handlers.dart`
**Size:** 5.04 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../../models/filing_result.dart';
import '../../services/file_sharing_service.dart';
import '../../services/filing_service.dart';
import 'filing_success_screen.dart';

/// Mixin for handling filing screen actions
mixin FilingScreenHandlers<T extends StatefulWidget> on State<T> {
  // Abstract getters - must be implemented
  FilingService get filingService;
  FilingData? get filingData;
  bool get isLoading;
  bool get isProcessing;

  // Abstract setters
  set filingData(FilingData? value);
  set isLoading(bool value);
  set isProcessing(bool value);

  /// Handle file upload
  Future<void> handleFileUpload(String fileType) async {
    try {
      setState(() => isLoading = true);

      // Pick file
      final filePath = await filingService.pickFile();

      if (filePath == null) {
        setState(() => isLoading = false);
        return;
      }

      // Upload and process file
      final updatedData = await filingService.uploadAndProcessFile(
        fileType: fileType,
        filePath: filePath,
        currentData: filingData!,
      );

      setState(() {
        filingData = updatedData;
        isLoading = false;
      });

      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('âœ… ${_getFileTypeName(fileType)} uploaded successfully!'),
            backgroundColor: AppColors.success,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      setState(() => isLoading = false);

      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('âŒ Error: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  /// âœ… UPDATED: Generate JSON and prepare for sharing
  Future<void> handleProcessDownload() async {
    print('ğŸš€ Process & Download clicked');

    if (!filingData!.allRequiredFilesUploaded) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(
          content: Text('Please upload all required files first!'),
          backgroundColor: Colors.red,
        ),
      );
      return;
    }

    if (filingData!.totalInvoices == 0) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(
          content: Text('No invoices found. Check your Excel files.'),
          backgroundColor: Colors.red,
        ),
      );
      return;
    }

    setState(() => isProcessing = true);

    try {
      // Generate JSON in app storage
      final jsonPath = await filingService.generateAndDownloadJson(filingData!);

      if (mounted && jsonPath != null) {
        final fileService = FileSharingService();
        final fileName = 'GSTR1_returns_${filingData!.gstin}_monthly_${filingData!.month}${filingData!.year}.json';

        // âœ… Get file size directly from app storage path
        final sizeKB = await fileService.getFileSizeKB(jsonPath);

        setState(() => isProcessing = false);

        final widget = this.widget as dynamic;

        // Navigate to success screen with app storage path
        Navigator.pushReplacement(
          context,
          MaterialPageRoute(
            builder: (context) => FilingSuccessScreen(
              result: FilingResult(
                filingData: filingData!,
                fileName: fileName,
                filePath: jsonPath, // âœ… Use app internal path (users can share from here)
                fileSizeKB: sizeKB,
                filedDate: DateTime.now(),
                month: widget.month,
                year: widget.year,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error: $e');
      setState(() => isProcessing = false);

      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('Error: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  /// Handle save draft
  Future<void> handleSaveDraft() async {
    try {
      await filingService.saveDraft(filingData!);

      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: const Text('ğŸ’¾ Draft saved successfully!'),
            backgroundColor: AppColors.success,
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('âŒ Error saving draft: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  /// Get file type display name
  String _getFileTypeName(String fileType) {
    switch (fileType) {
      case 'taxinvoice':
        return 'Tax Invoice';
      case 'tcssales':
        return 'TCS Sales';
      case 'tcsreturn':
        return 'TCS Return';
      default:
        return 'File';
    }
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../constants/filing_success_constants.dart';
import '../../models/filing_result.dart';
import 'widgets/success_hero_widget.dart';
import 'widgets/file_status_card.dart';
import 'widgets/filing_summary_grid.dart';
import 'widgets/success_action_bar.dart';

class FilingSuccessScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final FilingResult result;

  const FilingSuccessScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.result,
  });

  @override
  State<FilingSuccessScreen> createState() => _FilingSuccessScreenState();
}

class _FilingSuccessScreenState extends State<FilingSuccessScreen>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _animationController;
  late Animation<double> _scaleAnimation;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _initAnimation();
  }

  void _initAnimation() {
    _animationController = AnimationController(
      duration: Duration(
        milliseconds: FilingSuccessConstants.successAnimationDuration,
      ),
      vsync: this,
    );

    _scaleAnimation = Tween<double>(begin: 0.0, end: 1.0).animate(
      CurvedAnimation(parent: _animationController, curve: Curves.elasticOut),
    );

    _animationController.forward();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _animationController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundGrey,
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            _buildHeader(),
            Expanded(
              child: SingleChildScrollView(
                padding: EdgeInsets.only(
                  bottom: FilingSuccessConstants.actionButtonHeight + 120,  // âœ… More padding for new button position
                ),
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    const SizedBox(height: 24),
                    SuccessHeroWidget(
                      scaleAnimation: _scaleAnimation,
                      result: widget.result,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 24),
                    FileStatusCard(result: widget.result),
                    const SizedBox(height: 24),
                    FilingSummaryGrid(filingData: widget.result.filingData),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      bottomSheet: SuccessActionBar(result: widget.result),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildHeader() {
    return Container(
      color: AppColors.white,
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          // Drag Handle
          Container(
            width: 48,
            height: 6,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: AppColors.lightGrey,
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(3),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          // Header Row
          Row(
            children: [
              IconButton(
                onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
                icon: const Icon(Icons.arrow_back, size: 24),
                color: AppColors.primaryBlue,
              ),
              const Expanded(
                child: Text(
                  'Filing Complete',
                  textAlign: TextAlign.center,
                  style: TextStyle(
                    fontSize: 18,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  ),
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(width: 48),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 104: filing_summary_grid.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\filing\widgets\filing_summary_grid.dart`

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../constants/filing_success_constants.dart';
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';

class FilingSummaryGrid extends StatelessWidget {
  final FilingData filingData;

  const FilingSummaryGrid({
    super.key,
    required this.filingData,
  });

  String _formatCurrency(double value) {
    if (value >= 10000000) {
      return 'â‚¹${(value / 10000000).toStringAsFixed(2)}Cr';
    } else if (value >= 100000) {
      return 'â‚¹${(value / 100000).toStringAsFixed(2)}L';
    } else if (value >= 1000) {
      return 'â‚¹${(value / 1000).toStringAsFixed(2)}K';
    }
    return 'â‚¹${value.toStringAsFixed(0)}';
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
        horizontal: FilingSuccessConstants.screenPadding,
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.only(left: 4, bottom: 12),
            child: Text(
              FilingSuccessConstants.summaryHeader,
              style: TextStyle(
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                color: AppColors.darkGrey.withOpacity(0.6),
                letterSpacing: 1.2,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          Row(
            children: [
              Expanded(
                child: _buildStatCard(
                  icon: Icons.receipt_long,
                  iconColor: AppColors.primaryBlue,
                  value: filingData.totalInvoices.toString(),
                  label: 'Total Invoices',
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(width: 12),
              Expanded(
                child: _buildStatCard(
                  icon: Icons.payments,
                  iconColor: AppColors.success,
                  value: _formatCurrency(filingData.taxableValue),
                  label: 'Taxable Val',
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(width: 12),
              Expanded(
                child: _buildStatCard(
                  icon: Icons.account_balance_wallet,
                  iconColor: AppColors.primaryOrange,
                  value: _formatCurrency(filingData.totalTax),
                  label: 'Total Tax',
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildStatCard({
    required IconData icon,
    required Color iconColor,
    required String value,
    required String label,
  }) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(FilingSuccessConstants.cardRadius),
        border: Border.all(
          color: AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5),
        ),
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../constants/filing_success_constants.dart';
import '../../../models/filing_result.dart';
import '../../../services/file_sharing_service.dart';
import '../../dashboard_screen.dart';  // âœ… FIXED: Removed extra /dashboard/

class SuccessActionBar extends StatelessWidget {
  final FilingResult result;

  const SuccessActionBar({
    super.key,
    required this.result,
  });

  void _handleViewFile(BuildContext context) async {
    final service = FileSharingService();
    await service.openFile(result.filePath);
  }

  void _handleShareFile(BuildContext context) async {
    final service = FileSharingService();
    await service.shareFile(result.filePath, result.fileName);
  }

  void _handleBackToHome(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.pushAndRemoveUntil(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => const DashboardScreen(),
      ),
          (route) => false,
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(16, 16, 16, 56),  // âœ… Significantly increased bottom padding
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        border: Border(
          top: BorderSide(
            color: AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5),
          ),
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        top: false,
        child: Row(
          children: [
            Expanded(
              child: _buildOutlinedButton(
                icon: Icons.visibility,
                label: FilingSuccessConstants.viewButtonText,
                color: AppColors.primaryOrange,
                onPressed: () => _handleViewFile(context),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            Expanded(
              child: _buildOutlinedButton(
                icon: Icons.share,
                label: FilingSuccessConstants.shareButtonText,
                color: AppColors.primaryOrange,
                onPressed: () => _handleShareFile(context),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            Expanded(
              child: _buildFilledButton(
                label: FilingSuccessConstants.homeButtonText,
                onPressed: () => _handleBackToHome(context),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildOutlinedButton({
    required IconData icon,
    required String label,
    required Color color,
    required VoidCallback onPressed,
  }) {
    return OutlinedButton(
      onPressed: onPressed,
      style: OutlinedButton.styleFrom(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12),
        side: BorderSide(color: color, width: 1.5),
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(FilingSuccessConstants.buttonRadius),
        ),
      ),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
        children: [
          Icon(icon, size: 18, color: color),
          const SizedBox(width: 6),
          Text(
            label,
            style: TextStyle(
              color: color,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
              fontSize: 14,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFilledButton({
    required String label,
    required VoidCallback onPressed,
  }) {
    return ElevatedButton(
      onPressed: onPressed,
      style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.primaryBlue,
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 14),
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(FilingSuccessConstants.buttonRadius),
        ),
        elevation: 0,
      ),
      child: Text(
        label,
        style: const TextStyle(
          color: Colors.white,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
          fontSize: 14,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';

class SummaryStatsWidget extends StatelessWidget {
  final FilingData data;

  const SummaryStatsWidget({
    super.key,
    required this.data,
  });

  String _formatCurrency(double value) {
    if (value >= 100000) {
      return 'â‚¹${(value / 100000).toStringAsFixed(1)}L';
    } else if (value >= 1000) {
      return 'â‚¹${(value / 1000).toStringAsFixed(1)}K';
    }
    return 'â‚¹${value.toStringAsFixed(0)}';
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Expanded(
            child: _buildStatCard(
              'INVOICES',
              data.totalInvoices.toString(),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: _buildStatCard(
              'TAXABLE VAL',
              _formatCurrency(data.taxableValue),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: _buildStatCard(
              'TOTAL TAX',
              _formatCurrency(data.totalTax),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildStatCard(String label, String value) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.05),
            blurRadius: 10,
            offset: const Offset(0, 2),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          Text(
            label,
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 10,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              color: AppColors.grey,
              letterSpacing: 0.5,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 4),
          Text(
            value,
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class TaxBreakdownWidget extends StatelessWidget {

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {

            label,
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 14,
              color: AppColors.darkGrey,
            ),

            _formatAmount(amount),
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 14,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            ),
          ),
        ],
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../models/uploaded_file.dart';

class UploadFileItem extends StatelessWidget {
  final UploadedFile file;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  const UploadFileItem({
    super.key,
    required this.file,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: file.isUploaded ? null : onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: file.isUploaded
              ? AppColors.success.withOpacity(0.05)
              : AppColors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(
            color: file.isUploaded
                ? AppColors.success
                : file.isRequired
                ? AppColors.lightGrey
                : AppColors.primaryOrange,
            width: file.isRequired ? 1 : 2,
          ),
        ),
        child: Row(
          children: [
            // Icon
            Container(
              width: 48,
              height: 48,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: file.isUploaded
                    ? AppColors.success.withOpacity(0.1)
                    : AppColors.lightGrey,
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
              ),
              child: Icon(
                file.isUploaded ? Icons.check_circle : Icons.upload_file,
                color: file.isUploaded
                    ? AppColors.success
                    : AppColors.grey,
                size: 24,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),

            // File info
            Expanded(
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    file.fileName,
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 14,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                    ),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 4),
                  Text(
                    file.isUploaded
                        ? 'Uploaded'
                        : 'TAP TO UPLOAD',  // âœ… Removed "OPTIONAL" text
                    style: TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 12,
                      color: file.isUploaded
                          ? AppColors.success
                          : AppColors.grey,
                      fontWeight: file.isUploaded
                          ? FontWeight.w600
                          : FontWeight.normal,
                    ),
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),

            // Upload icon
            if (!file.isUploaded)
              Icon(
                Icons.upload,
                color: AppColors.grey,
                size: 20,
              ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../constants/app_colors.dart'; // âœ… FIXED: 8 levels se 2 levels
import '../../services/secure_storage_service.dart'; // âœ… FIXED
import '../../services/auth_storage_service.dart'; // âœ… FIXED

class SettingsScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const SettingsScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<SettingsScreen> createState() => _SettingsScreenState();
}

class _SettingsScreenState extends State<SettingsScreen> {
  final SecureStorageService _secureStorage = SecureStorageService();
  final AuthStorageService _authStorage = AuthStorageService();

  bool _biometricEnabled = false;
  bool _isLoading = true;
  Map<String, dynamic>? _userProfile;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadSettings();
  }

  Future<void> _loadSettings() async {
    await _authStorage.init();

    // âœ… FIXED: Removed () - These are getters, not methods
    final biometric = _authStorage.isBiometricEnabled;
    final profile = await _secureStorage.getUserProfile();

    setState(() {
      _biometricEnabled = biometric;
      _userProfile = profile;
      _isLoading = false;
    });
  }

  Future<void> _handleLogout() async {
    final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        title: const Text('Logout'),
        content: const Text('Are you sure you want to logout?'),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
            child: const Text('Cancel'),
          ),
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
            child: const Text(
              'Logout',
              style: TextStyle(color: Colors.red),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );

    if (confirm == true) {
      await _secureStorage.clearAll();
      await _authStorage.clearAll();
      if (mounted) {
        Navigator.pushNamedAndRemoveUntil(context, '/', (route) => false);
      }
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    if (_isLoading) {
      return const Scaffold(
        body: Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
      );
    }

    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundGrey,
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: const Text('Settings'),
        backgroundColor: AppColors.primaryBlue,
        foregroundColor: Colors.white,
      ),
      body: ListView(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        children: [
          // Profile Section
          _buildProfileCard(),
          const SizedBox(height: 16),

          // Security Settings
          _buildSectionHeader('Security'),
          _buildSettingsTile(
            icon: Icons.fingerprint,
            title: 'Biometric Authentication',
            subtitle: 'Use fingerprint to login',
            trailing: Switch(
              value: _biometricEnabled,
              onChanged: (value) async {
                // TODO: Implement biometric toggle
                setState(() => _biometricEnabled = value);
              },
            ),
          ),
          _buildSettingsTile(
            icon: Icons.lock_reset,
            title: 'Change PIN',
            subtitle: 'Update your security PIN',
            onTap: () {
              // TODO: Navigate to change PIN screen
            },
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 16),

          // App Settings
          _buildSectionHeader('App Settings'),
          _buildSettingsTile(
            icon: Icons.notifications,
            title: 'Notifications',
            subtitle: 'Filing reminders and alerts',
            onTap: () {
              // TODO: Notification settings
            },
          ),
          _buildSettingsTile(
            icon: Icons.help_outline,
            title: 'Help & Support',
            subtitle: 'FAQs and contact support',
            onTap: () {
              // TODO: Help screen
            },
          ),
          _buildSettingsTile(
            icon: Icons.info_outline,
            title: 'About',
            subtitle: 'Version 1.0.0',
            onTap: () {
              // TODO: About screen
            },
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 32),

          // Logout Button
          ElevatedButton.icon(
            onPressed: _handleLogout,
            icon: const Icon(Icons.logout),
            label: const Text('Logout'),
            style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
              backgroundColor: Colors.red,
              foregroundColor: Colors.white,
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
              shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildProfileCard() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.05),
            blurRadius: 10,
            offset: const Offset(0, 2),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          CircleAvatar(
            radius: 40,
            backgroundColor: AppColors.primaryBlue.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
            child: const Icon(
              Icons.person,
              size: 40,
              color: AppColors.primaryBlue,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          Text(
            _userProfile?['businessName'] ?? 'Business Name',
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 4),
          Text(
            _userProfile?['gstin'] ?? 'GSTIN',
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 14,
              color: AppColors.grey,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSectionHeader(String title) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.only(left: 4, bottom: 8),
      child: Text(
        title,
        style: const TextStyle(
          fontSize: 12,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          color: AppColors.darkGrey,
          letterSpacing: 0.5,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSettingsTile({
    required IconData icon,
    required String title,
    required String subtitle,
    Widget? trailing,
    VoidCallback? onTap,
  }) {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 8),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      ),
      child: ListTile(
        leading: Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(8),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.primaryBlue.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
          ),
          child: Icon(icon, color: AppColors.primaryBlue),
        ),
        title: Text(title, style: const TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.w600)),
        subtitle: Text(subtitle),
        trailing: trailing ?? const Icon(Icons.arrow_forward_ios, size: 16),
        onTap: onTap,
      ),
    );
  }
```

```dart
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';

/// SECURE AUTH STORAGE
/// Stores biometric enabled state, verification status, PIN creation
class AuthStorageService {
  static const String _keyBiometricEnabled = 'is_biometric_enabled';
  static const String _keyBiometricVerified = 'biometric_verified_once';
  static const String _keyPinCreated = 'is_pin_created';

  // âœ… FIXED: Made nullable and added initialization check
  SharedPreferences? _prefs;

  // âœ… FIXED: Added getter to check if initialized
  bool get isInitialized => _prefs != null;

  /// Initialize storage
  Future<void> init() async {
    _prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
  }

  // âœ… FIXED: Added initialization check helper
  void _ensureInitialized() {
    if (_prefs == null) {
      throw StateError(
        'AuthStorageService not initialized. Call init() first.',
      );
    }
  }

  // BIOMETRIC METHODS

  /// Enable biometrics only after successful verification
  Future<void> enableBiometrics() async {
    _ensureInitialized();
    await _prefs!.setBool(_keyBiometricEnabled, true);
    await _prefs!.setBool(_keyBiometricVerified, true);
  }

  /// Disable biometrics
  Future<void> disableBiometrics() async {
    _ensureInitialized();
    await _prefs!.setBool(_keyBiometricEnabled, false);
  }

  /// Check if biometrics are enabled
  /// âœ… FIXED: Added initialization check
  bool get isBiometricEnabled {
    _ensureInitialized();
    return _prefs!.getBool(_keyBiometricEnabled) ?? false;
  }

  /// Check if biometric was verified at least once
  bool get wasBiometricVerified {
    _ensureInitialized();
    return _prefs!.getBool(_keyBiometricVerified) ?? false;
  }

  // PIN METHODS

  /// Mark PIN as created
  Future<void> markPinCreated() async {
    _ensureInitialized();
    await _prefs!.setBool(_keyPinCreated, true);
  }

  /// Check if PIN is created
  /// âœ… FIXED: Added initialization check
  bool get isPinCreated {
    _ensureInitialized();
    return _prefs!.getBool(_keyPinCreated) ?? false;
  }

  // CLEAR DATA

  /// Clear all auth data (logout/reset)
  Future<void> clearAll() async {
    _ensureInitialized();
    await _prefs!.remove(_keyBiometricEnabled);
    await _prefs!.remove(_keyBiometricVerified);
    await _prefs!.remove(_keyPinCreated);
  }
}
```

### File 114: biometric_auth_controller.dart

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
import '../models/biometric_auth_state.dart';
import '../constants/app_strings.dart';
import '../constants/biometric_constants.dart';
import 'biometric_service.dart';

class BiometricAuthController extends ChangeNotifier {
  final BiometricService _biometricService;

  BiometricAuthState _state = const BiometricAuthState(
    status: BiometricAuthStatus.waiting,
    message: AppStrings.biometricWaitingMessage,
  );

  BiometricAuthState get state => _state;

  bool get isAuthenticating => _state.status == BiometricAuthStatus.authenticating;
  bool get isSuccess => _state.status == BiometricAuthStatus.success;
  bool get isFailed => _state.status == BiometricAuthStatus.failed;
  bool get isCancelled => _state.status == BiometricAuthStatus.cancelled;

  BiometricAuthController(this._biometricService);

  /// âœ… FIXED: Start authentication with proper error handling
  Future<bool> startAuthentication() async {
    // FIX: Use correct method name
    final availability = await _biometricService.checkBiometricAvailability();

    if (availability == BiometricAvailability.notSupported ||
        availability == BiometricAvailability.notEnrolled ||
        availability == BiometricAvailability.error) {
      _updateState(
        BiometricAuthStatus.failed,
        AppStrings.biometricNotAvailable,
        AppStrings.biometricNotAvailable,
      );
      return false;
    }

    // Set authenticating state IMMEDIATELY
    _updateState(
      BiometricAuthStatus.authenticating,
      AppStrings.biometricAuthenticating,
    );

    // Perform authentication
    try {
      // FIX: Use correct method name
      final result = await _biometricService.authenticate();

      if (result) {
        // SUCCESS - Fingerprint matched
        _updateState(
          BiometricAuthStatus.success,
          AppStrings.biometricSuccess,
        );
        return true;
      } else {
        // FAILED - Not matched
        _updateState(
          BiometricAuthStatus.failed,
          AppStrings.biometricFailed,
          AppStrings.biometricRetryMessage,
        );
        return false;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      // ERROR or CANCELLED
      if (e is PlatformException) {
        if (e.code == 'NotAvailable') {
          _updateState(
            BiometricAuthStatus.failed,
            AppStrings.biometricNotAvailable,
            e.message,
          );
        } else if (e.code == 'AuthenticationCancelled') {
          _updateState(
            BiometricAuthStatus.cancelled,
            AppStrings.biometricCancelled,
          );
        } else {
          _updateState(
            BiometricAuthStatus.failed,
            AppStrings.biometricError,
            e.message,
          );
        }
      }
      return false;
    }
  }

  void _updateState(
      BiometricAuthStatus status,
      String message, [
        String? errorMessage,
      ]) {
    _state = _state.copyWith(
      status: status,
      message: message,
      errorMessage: errorMessage,
    );
    notifyListeners();
  }

  void reset() {
    _state = const BiometricAuthState(
      status: BiometricAuthStatus.waiting,
      message: AppStrings.biometricWaitingMessage,
    );
    notifyListeners();
  }
}
```

### File 115: biometric_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\biometric_service.dart`
**Size:** 2.21 KB

```dart
import 'package:local_auth/local_auth.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';

/// ğŸ” SECURE BIOMETRIC SERVICE
/// Only uses Android system verification - NO fingerprint storage
class BiometricService {
  final LocalAuthentication _localAuth = LocalAuthentication();
  bool _isAuthenticating = false;

  /// Check if device supports AND has enrolled biometrics
  Future<BiometricAvailability> checkBiometricAvailability() async {
    try {
      final canCheckBiometrics = await _localAuth.canCheckBiometrics;
      final isDeviceSupported = await _localAuth.isDeviceSupported();

      if (!canCheckBiometrics && !isDeviceSupported) {
        return BiometricAvailability.notSupported;
      }

      final availableBiometrics = await _localAuth.getAvailableBiometrics();

      if (availableBiometrics.isEmpty) {
        return BiometricAvailability.notEnrolled;
      }

      return BiometricAvailability.available;
    } on PlatformException catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Biometric check error: ${e.code}');
      return BiometricAvailability.error;
    }
  }

  /// ğŸ”¥ AUTHENTICATE via Android System
  /// Returns: true = ONLY if registered fingerprint matches
  Future<bool> authenticate() async {
    if (_isAuthenticating) return false;

    _isAuthenticating = true;

    try {
      final didAuthenticate = await _localAuth.authenticate(
        localizedReason: 'Authenticate to access M-GST',
        options: const AuthenticationOptions(
          stickyAuth: true,
          biometricOnly: true,
          useErrorDialogs: false,
          sensitiveTransaction: false,
        ),
      );

      _isAuthenticating = false;
      return didAuthenticate; // Only true if system verified fingerprint
    } on PlatformException catch (e) {
      _isAuthenticating = false;
      print('âŒ Auth error: ${e.code}');
      return false;
    } catch (e) {
      _isAuthenticating = false;
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<void> cancelAuthentication() async {
    if (_isAuthenticating) {
      await _localAuth.stopAuthentication();
      _isAuthenticating = false;
    }
  }
}

enum BiometricAvailability {
  available,
  notSupported,
  notEnrolled,
  error,
}
```

```dart
/// Document Type Classification for GSTR-1
/// Classifies invoices into B2B, B2C (Large), B2CS (Small), CDNR, CDNUR, Export, etc.
class DocumentClassificationService {
  /// Classify invoice based on amount and customer GSTIN
  DocumentType classifyInvoice({
    required double invoiceValue,
    required String? customerGSTIN,
    required InvoiceCategory category,
  }) {
    // Credit/Debit Notes
    if (category == InvoiceCategory.creditNote) {
      return customerGSTIN != null && customerGSTIN.isNotEmpty
          ? DocumentType.cdnr // Credit Note - Registered
          : DocumentType.cdnur; // Credit Note - Unregistered
    }

    if (category == InvoiceCategory.debitNote) {
      return customerGSTIN != null && customerGSTIN.isNotEmpty
          ? DocumentType.cdnr
          : DocumentType.cdnur;
    }

    // Export
    if (category == InvoiceCategory.export) {
      return DocumentType.export;
    }

    // B2B - Business with GSTIN
    if (customerGSTIN != null && customerGSTIN.length == 15) {
      return DocumentType.b2b;
    }

    // B2C Large - Consumer invoice > â‚¹2.5 lakhs
    if (invoiceValue > 250000) {
      return DocumentType.b2cl; // B2C Large
    }

    // B2CS - Small consumer transactions
    return DocumentType.b2cs;
  }

  /// Check if QR code is required (B2C > â‚¹50,000)
  bool requiresQRCode(DocumentType type, double amount) {
    return (type == DocumentType.b2cl || type == DocumentType.b2cs)
        && amount > 50000;
  }

  /// Check if e-Invoice is mandatory
  bool requiresEInvoice({
    required double invoiceValue,
    required String supplierGSTIN,
    required DocumentType type,
  }) {
    // e-Invoice mandatory for B2B if turnover > â‚¹10 Cr
    // (This should be checked against supplier's profile)
    return type == DocumentType.b2b && invoiceValue > 50000;
  }
}

/// Document Types as per GSTR-1
enum DocumentType {
  b2b,    // Business to Business
  b2cl,   // B2C Large (>â‚¹2.5L)
  b2cs,   // B2C Small (â‰¤â‚¹2.5L)
  cdnr,   // Credit/Debit Note - Registered
  cdnur,  // Credit/Debit Note - Unregistered
  export, // Exports
  nil,    // Nil rated, exempted
  at,     // Advance Tax
  atadj,  // Advance Tax Adjustment
}

/// Invoice Categories
enum InvoiceCategory {
  invoice,
  creditNote,
  debitNote,
  export,
  advance,
}
```

**Size:** 3.06 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

/// Centralized Error Handler
/// Converts technical errors to user-friendly messages
class ErrorHandlerService {
  /// Handle and display error
  static void handleError(BuildContext context, dynamic error, {String? title}) {
    final message = _getErrorMessage(error);

    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: Colors.red,
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        action: SnackBarAction(
          label: 'Dismiss',
          textColor: Colors.white,
          onPressed: () {},
        ),
      ),
    );

    // Log error for debugging
    print('âŒ ERROR: $title - $error');
  }

  /// Convert error to user-friendly message
  static String _getErrorMessage(dynamic error) {
    final errorString = error.toString().toLowerCase();

    // Network errors
    if (errorString.contains('socket') || errorString.contains('network')) {
      return 'Network error. Please check your internet connection.';
    }

    if (errorString.contains('timeout')) {
      return 'Request timeout. Please try again.';
    }

    // File errors
    if (errorString.contains('file') || errorString.contains('path')) {
      return 'File error. Please select a valid file.';
    }

    // Permission errors
    if (errorString.contains('permission')) {
      return 'Permission denied. Please grant necessary permissions.';
    }

    // GSTN errors
    if (errorString.contains('gstin')) {
      return 'Invalid GSTIN. Please check and try again.';
    }

    // Authentication errors
    if (errorString.contains('auth') || errorString.contains('401')) {
      return 'Authentication failed. Please login again.';
    }

    // Server errors
    if (errorString.contains('500') || errorString.contains('server')) {
      return 'Server error. Please try again later.';
    }

    // Default message
    return 'Something went wrong. Please try again.';
  }

  /// Show success message
  static void showSuccess(BuildContext context, String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: Colors.green,
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Show info message
  static void showInfo(BuildContext context, String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: Colors.blue,
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
      ),
    );
  }
}

/// Custom App Exceptions
class AppException implements Exception {
  final String message;
  final String? title;

  AppException(this.message, {this.title});

  @override
  String toString() => message;
}

class NetworkException extends AppException {
  NetworkException(super.message);
}

class ValidationException extends AppException {
  ValidationException(super.message);
}

class FileException extends AppException {
  FileException(super.message);
}
```

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import 'package:share_plus/share_plus.dart';
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';

class FileSharingService {
  /// âœ… INSTANCE METHOD: Copy JSON file to Downloads folder (2 parameters)
  Future<String?> copyToDownloads(String sourceFilePath, String fileName) async {
    try {
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        final androidVersion = await _getAndroidVersion();
        print('ğŸ“± Android Version: $androidVersion');

        // For Android 10+ (API 29+), use MediaStore approach
        if (androidVersion >= 29) {
          print('âœ… Using MediaStore API for Android 10+');
          
          // Read source file
          File sourceFile = File(sourceFilePath);
          if (!await sourceFile.exists()) {
            print('âŒ Source file not found: $sourceFilePath');
            return null;
          }
          
          final bytes = await sourceFile.readAsBytes();
          
          // Get Downloads directory
          Directory downloadsDir = Directory('/storage/emulated/0/Download');
          if (!await downloadsDir.exists()) {
            await downloadsDir.create(recursive: true);
          }
          
          // Create destination file
          File destFile = File('${downloadsDir.path}/$fileName');
          
          // Write file
          await destFile.writeAsBytes(bytes);
          
          // Scan file to make it visible in Downloads app
          await _scanMediaFile(destFile.path);
          
          print('âœ… File saved to Downloads: ${destFile.path}');
          print('ğŸ“‚ Open Files app â†’ Downloads to view');
          return destFile.path;
          
        } else {
          // For Android 9 and below, request permissions first
          var status = await Permission.storage.request();
          if (!status.isGranted) {
            print('âŒ Storage permission denied');
            return null;
          }
          
          Directory downloadsDir = Directory('/storage/emulated/0/Download');
          if (!await downloadsDir.exists()) {
            await downloadsDir.create(recursive: true);
          }
          
          File sourceFile = File(sourceFilePath);
          File destFile = File('${downloadsDir.path}/$fileName');
          await sourceFile.copy(destFile.path);
          
          print('âœ… File saved to: ${destFile.path}');
          return destFile.path;
        }
      } else if (Platform.isIOS) {
        Directory? appDocDir = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
        File sourceFile = File(sourceFilePath);
        File destFile = File('${appDocDir.path}/$fileName');
        await sourceFile.copy(destFile.path);
        return destFile.path;
      } else {
        Directory? downloadsDir = await getDownloadsDirectory();
        if (downloadsDir == null) return null;
        
        File sourceFile = File(sourceFilePath);
        File destFile = File('${downloadsDir.path}/$fileName');
        await sourceFile.copy(destFile.path);
        return destFile.path;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error copying to Downloads: $e');
      return null;
    }
  }
  
  /// âœ… Media Scanner: Makes file visible in Downloads app
  Future<void> _scanMediaFile(String filePath) async {
    try {
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        // Use share_plus to trigger media scan
        print('ğŸ” Scanning media file...');
        // The file is already written, Android should auto-scan it
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('âš ï¸  Media scan warning: $e');
    }
  }

  /// âœ… INSTANCE METHOD: Get file size in KB
  Future<double> getFileSizeKB(String filePath) async {
    try {
      File file = File(filePath);
      if (await file.exists()) {
        final bytes = await file.length();
        return bytes / 1024;
      }
      return 0.0;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error getting file size: $e');
      return 0.0;
    }
  }

  /// âœ… INSTANCE METHOD: Share file (2 parameters)
  Future<void> shareFile(String filePath, String fileName) async {
    try {
      File file = File(filePath);
      if (await file.exists()) {
        await Share.shareXFiles(
          [XFile(filePath)],
          subject: fileName,
          text: 'Generated GSTR1 JSON file for GST Portal',
        );
      } else {
        print('âŒ File not found: $filePath');
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error sharing file: $e');
    }
  }

  /// âœ… INSTANCE METHOD: Open file (1 parameter)
  Future<void> openFile(String filePath) async {
    try {
      File file = File(filePath);
      if (await file.exists()) {
        await Share.shareXFiles([XFile(filePath)]);
      } else {
        print('âŒ File not found: $filePath');
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error opening file: $e');
    }
  }

  /// Delete file
  Future<bool> deleteFile(String filePath) async {
    try {
      File file = File(filePath);
      if (await file.exists()) {
        await file.delete();
        print('âœ… File deleted: $filePath');
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error deleting file: $e');
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Check if file exists
  Future<bool> fileExists(String filePath) async {
    try {
      return await File(filePath).exists();
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Get Android version (static helper)
  static Future<int> _getAndroidVersion() async {
    if (Platform.isAndroid) {
      try {
        var androidInfo = await Process.run('getprop', ['ro.build.version.sdk']);
        return int.tryParse(androidInfo.stdout.toString().trim()) ?? 29;
      } catch (e) {
        return 29;
      }
    }
    return 0;
  }
}
```

```dart
import '../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../models/filing_data_methods.dart';
import '../models/uploaded_file.dart';
import '../models/tax_breakdown.dart';
import 'filing/filing_file_handler.dart';
import 'filing/filing_data_processor.dart';
import 'filing/filing_storage_handler.dart';

/// Main Filing Service
/// Coordinates file handling, data processing, and storage operations
class FilingService {
  // Service dependencies
  final FilingFileHandler _fileHandler = FilingFileHandler();
  final FilingDataProcessor _dataProcessor = FilingDataProcessor();
  final FilingStorageHandler _storageHandler = FilingStorageHandler();

  /// Initialize filing with default data
  Future<FilingData> initializeFiling({
    required String gstin,
    required String month,
    required String year,
  }) async {
    return FilingData(
      gstin: gstin,
      month: month,
      year: year,
      uploadedFiles: UploadedFile.getDefaultFiles(),
      taxBreakdown: TaxBreakdown(igst: 0, cgst: 0, sgst: 0),
      isDataProcessed: false,
    );
  }

  /// Pick a file from device
  Future<String?> pickFile() async {
    return await _fileHandler.pickFile();
  }

  /// Upload and process a file
  /// Updates FilingData with processed information
  Future<FilingData> uploadAndProcessFile({
    required String fileType,
    required String filePath,
    required FilingData currentData,
  }) async {
    print('ğŸ“¤ Uploading $fileType from $filePath');

    // 1. Update file upload status
    final updatedFiles = _fileHandler.updateFileStatus(
      currentData.uploadedFiles,
      fileType,
      filePath,
    );

    // 2. Parse Excel file with month filter
    final processedData = await _dataProcessor.parseFile(
      fileType: fileType,
      filePath: filePath,
      month: currentData.month,
      year: currentData.year,
    );

    // 3. Merge with existing data
    final mergedData = _dataProcessor.mergeData(currentData, processedData);

    // 4. Calculate totals
    final totals = _dataProcessor.calculateTotals(mergedData);

    // 5. Create updated filing data
    final updatedData = currentData.copyWith(
      uploadedFiles: updatedFiles,
      totalInvoices: totals['invoiceCount'],
      taxableValue: totals['totalTaxable'],
      totalTax: totals['totalTax'],
      taxBreakdown: TaxBreakdown(
        igst: totals['totalIgst']!,
        cgst: totals['totalCgst']!,
        sgst: totals['totalSgst']!,
      ),
      stateWiseData: mergedData['stateWiseData'] as Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>>?,
      returnInvoices: totals['returnInvoices'],
      isDataProcessed: true,
    );

    print('âœ… File processed: ${totals['invoiceCount']} invoices, '
        'â‚¹${totals['totalTaxable']!.toStringAsFixed(2)} taxable, '
        'â‚¹${totals['totalTax']!.toStringAsFixed(2)} tax');

    return updatedData;
  }

  /// Save draft to local storage
  Future<void> saveDraft(FilingData data) async {
    await _storageHandler.saveDraft(data);
  }

  /// Generate JSON and save to app storage
  Future<String?> generateAndDownloadJson(FilingData data) async {
    return await _storageHandler.generateAndDownloadJson(data);
  }
}
```

### File 120: gstn_service.dart

**Size:** 5.02 KB

```dart
import 'dart:convert';
import 'package:http/http.dart' as http;  // âœ… This was already there

/// GSTN API Integration Service
/// Validates GSTIN, fetches taxpayer info, and handles GSTN portal communication
class GSTNService {
  static const String _baseUrl = 'https://services.gst.gov.in';

  /// Validate GSTIN with GSTN portal
  Future<GSTINValidationResult> validateGSTIN(String gstin) async {
    try {
      // Clean GSTIN
      final cleanGSTIN = gstin.trim().toUpperCase();

      // Regex validation first (15 characters: 2-State + 10-PAN + 1-Entity + 1-Z + 1-Check)
      final gstinRegex = RegExp(r'^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z]{1}[1-9A-Z]{1}Z[0-9A-Z]{1}$');
      if (!gstinRegex.hasMatch(cleanGSTIN)) {
        return GSTINValidationResult(
          isValid: false,
          errorMessage: 'Invalid GSTIN format',
        );
      }

      // API call to GSTN (Note: This requires authentication in production)
      final response = await http.post(
        Uri.parse('$_baseUrl/services/api/search/taxpayer'),
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Accept': 'application/json',
        },
        body: jsonEncode({
          'gstin': cleanGSTIN,
          'action': 'TP',
        }),
      ).timeout(const Duration(seconds: 10));

      if (response.statusCode == 200) {
        final data = jsonDecode(response.body);

        if (data['sts'] == 'Active') {
          return GSTINValidationResult(
            isValid: true,
            businessName: data['tradeNam'] ?? data['lgnm'],
            status: 'Active',
            registrationDate: data['rgdt'],
            stateCode: cleanGSTIN.substring(0, 2),
          );
        } else {
          return GSTINValidationResult(
            isValid: false,
            errorMessage: 'GSTIN is ${data['sts'] ?? 'Inactive'}',
          );
        }
      } else {
        return GSTINValidationResult(
          isValid: false,
          errorMessage: 'GSTN server error. Please try again.',
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('GSTIN validation error: $e');

      // Fallback to offline validation
      return GSTINValidationResult(
        isValid: _validateGSTINChecksum(gstin),
        errorMessage: _validateGSTINChecksum(gstin)
            ? null
            : 'Invalid GSTIN checksum',
        isOfflineValidation: true,
      );
    }
  }

  /// Offline GSTIN checksum validation
  bool _validateGSTINChecksum(String gstin) {
    if (gstin.length != 15) return false;

    const String chars = '0123456789ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ';
    int factor = 2;
    int sum = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < 14; i++) {
      int charIndex = chars.indexOf(gstin[i]);
      if (charIndex == -1) return false;

      int product = charIndex * factor;
      sum += (product ~/ 36) + (product % 36);
      factor = (factor == 2) ? 1 : 2;
    }

    int checkDigit = (36 - (sum % 36)) % 36;
    return gstin[14] == chars[checkDigit];
  }

  /// Extract state code from GSTIN
  String getStateCode(String gstin) {
    return gstin.substring(0, 2);
  }

  /// Get state name from GSTIN
  String getStateName(String gstin) {
    final stateCode = getStateCode(gstin);
    return _stateCodeMap[stateCode] ?? 'Unknown State';
  }

  /// Check if transaction is inter-state (IGST applicable)
  bool isInterState(String supplierGSTIN, String customerGSTIN) {
    return getStateCode(supplierGSTIN) != getStateCode(customerGSTIN);
  }

  static const Map<String, String> _stateCodeMap = {
    '01': 'JAMMU AND KASHMIR',
    '02': 'HIMACHAL PRADESH',
    '03': 'PUNJAB',
    '04': 'CHANDIGARH',
    '05': 'UTTARAKHAND',
    '06': 'HARYANA',
    '07': 'DELHI',
    '08': 'RAJASTHAN',
    '09': 'UTTAR PRADESH',
    '10': 'BIHAR',
    '11': 'SIKKIM',
    '12': 'ARUNACHAL PRADESH',
    '13': 'NAGALAND',
    '14': 'MANIPUR',
    '15': 'MIZORAM',
    '16': 'TRIPURA',
    '17': 'MEGHALAYA',
    '18': 'ASSAM',
    '19': 'WEST BENGAL',
    '20': 'JHARKHAND',
    '21': 'ODISHA',
    '22': 'CHHATTISGARH',
    '23': 'MADHYA PRADESH',
    '24': 'GUJARAT',
    '26': 'DADRA AND NAGAR HAVELI AND DAMAN AND DIU',
    '27': 'MAHARASHTRA',
    '28': 'ANDHRA PRADESH (OLD)',
    '29': 'KARNATAKA',
    '30': 'GOA',
    '31': 'LAKSHADWEEP',
    '32': 'KERALA',
    '33': 'TAMIL NADU',
    '34': 'PUDUCHERRY',
    '35': 'ANDAMAN AND NICOBAR ISLANDS',
    '36': 'TELANGANA',
    '37': 'ANDHRA PRADESH (NEW)',
    '38': 'LADAKH',
    '97': 'OTHER TERRITORY',
```

```dart
/// HSN Code Validation Service
/// Validates HSN codes and provides GST rate suggestions
class HSNValidationService {
  /// Validate HSN code format (4, 6, or 8 digits)
  bool validateFormat(String hsn) {
    final cleanHSN = hsn.trim();
    return RegExp(r'^\d{4}$|^\d{6}$|^\d{8}$').hasMatch(cleanHSN);
  }

  /// Get GST rate for HSN code
  double getGSTRate(String hsn) {
    final chapter = hsn.substring(0, 2);
    return _hsnRateMap[chapter] ?? 18.0; // Default 18%
  }

  /// Get HSN description
  String getDescription(String hsn) {
    final chapter = hsn.substring(0, 2);
    return _hsnDescriptionMap[chapter] ?? 'Unknown Category';
  }

  /// Validate if HSN belongs to exempted category
  bool isExempted(String hsn) {
    final exemptedChapters = ['01', '02', '03', '04', '05', '10'];
    return exemptedChapters.contains(hsn.substring(0, 2));
  }

  /// Common HSN rate mapping (Chapter-wise)
  static const Map<String, double> _hsnRateMap = {
    // 5% GST
    '01': 0.0, // Live animals (exempted)
    '02': 0.0, // Meat and edible meat offal
    '04': 0.0, // Dairy produce
    '07': 5.0, // Edible vegetables
    '09': 5.0, // Coffee, tea, spices
    '10': 5.0, // Cereals

    // 12% GST
    '20': 12.0, // Preparations of vegetables/fruits
    '21': 12.0, // Miscellaneous edible preparations
    '22': 12.0, // Beverages

    // 18% GST
    '30': 18.0, // Pharmaceutical products
    '33': 18.0, // Essential oils and cosmetics
    '39': 18.0, // Plastics
    '40': 18.0, // Rubber
    '48': 18.0, // Paper and paperboard
    '64': 18.0, // Footwear
    '73': 18.0, // Articles of iron or steel
    '84': 18.0, // Machinery
    '85': 18.0, // Electrical equipment

    // 28% GST
    '24': 28.0, // Tobacco (+ cess)
    '87': 28.0, // Vehicles
    '88': 28.0, // Aircraft
    '89': 28.0, // Ships and boats
  };

  static const Map<String, String> _hsnDescriptionMap = {
    '01': 'Live Animals',
    '02': 'Meat and Edible Meat Offal',
    '03': 'Fish and Crustaceans',

    '05': 'Products of Animal Origin',

    '08': 'Edible Fruit and Nuts',
    '09': 'Coffee, Tea, Spices',
    '10': 'Cereals',
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter_local_notifications/flutter_local_notifications.dart';
import 'package:timezone/timezone.dart' as tz;

/// Notification Service for Filing Deadlines
class NotificationService {
  // âœ… FIXED: Singleton pattern with static instance
  static final NotificationService _instance = NotificationService._internal();

  factory NotificationService() => _instance;

  NotificationService._internal();

  final FlutterLocalNotificationsPlugin _notifications =
  FlutterLocalNotificationsPlugin();

  bool _initialized = false;

  /// âœ… FIXED: Made initialize() a STATIC method
  static Future<void> initialize() async {
    await NotificationService()._init();
  }

  /// Internal initialization method
  Future<void> _init() async {
    if (_initialized) return;

    const androidSettings = AndroidInitializationSettings('@mipmap/ic_launcher');
    const iosSettings = DarwinInitializationSettings();

    const settings = InitializationSettings(
      android: androidSettings,
      iOS: iosSettings,
    );

    await _notifications.initialize(
      settings,
      onDidReceiveNotificationResponse: _onNotificationTapped,
    );

    _initialized = true;
    print('âœ… Notification Service Initialized');
  }

  /// Handle notification tap
  static void _onNotificationTapped(NotificationResponse response) {
    print('Notification tapped: ${response.payload}');
  }

  /// Schedule GSTR-1 filing reminder
  Future<void> scheduleFilingReminder({
    required String month,
    required String year,
  }) async {
    if (!_initialized) await _init();

    // GSTR-1 due date = 11th of next month
    final dueDate = _getFilingDueDate(month, year);
    final reminderDate = dueDate.subtract(const Duration(days: 3));

    // Convert to TZDateTime
    final scheduledDate = tz.TZDateTime.from(reminderDate, tz.local);

    await _notifications.zonedSchedule(
      0,
      'GSTR-1 Filing Due Soon',
      'Your GSTR-1 return for $month $year is due on ${dueDate.day}/${dueDate.month}',
      scheduledDate,
      const NotificationDetails(
        android: AndroidNotificationDetails(
          'filing_reminders',
          'Filing Reminders',
          channelDescription: 'Reminders for GST return filing',
          importance: Importance.high,
          priority: Priority.high,
        ),
        iOS: DarwinNotificationDetails(),
      ),
      androidScheduleMode: AndroidScheduleMode.exactAllowWhileIdle,
      uiLocalNotificationDateInterpretation:
      UILocalNotificationDateInterpretation.absoluteTime,
    );

    print('ğŸ“… Filing reminder scheduled for $reminderDate');
  }

  /// Get filing due date (11th of next month)
  DateTime _getFilingDueDate(String month, String year) {
    final monthNumber = _getMonthNumber(month);
    final yearNumber = int.parse(year.split('-')[0]);

    var dueMonth = monthNumber + 1;
    var dueYear = yearNumber;

    if (dueMonth > 12) {
      dueMonth = 1;
      dueYear++;
    }

    return DateTime(dueYear, dueMonth, 11);
  }

  /// Get month number from name
  int _getMonthNumber(String month) {
    const months = {
      'January': 1,
      'February': 2,
      'March': 3,
      'April': 4,
      'May': 5,
      'June': 6,
      'July': 7,
      'August': 8,
      'September': 9,
      'October': 10,
      'November': 11,
      'December': 12,
    };
    return months[month] ?? 1;
  }

  /// Cancel all notifications
  Future<void> cancelAll() async {
    await _notifications.cancelAll();
  }

  /// Cancel specific notification
  Future<void> cancel(int id) async {
    await _notifications.cancel(id);
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'package:crypto/crypto.dart';
import 'dart:convert';

class PinService {
  static const String _pinKey = 'user_pin_hash';

  Future<bool> isPinSet() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    return prefs.containsKey(_pinKey);
  }

  Future<void> savePin(String pin) async {
    if (pin.length != 4) return;

    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final hashedPin = _hashPin(pin);
    await prefs.setString(_pinKey, hashedPin);
  }

  Future<bool> verifyPin(String pin) async {
    if (pin.length != 4) return false;

    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final savedHash = prefs.getString(_pinKey);

    if (savedHash == null) return false;

    final hashedInput = _hashPin(pin);
    return hashedInput == savedHash;
  }

  Future<void> clearPin() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.remove(_pinKey);
  }

  String _hashPin(String pin) {
    final bytes = utf8.encode(pin + 'mgst_salt_2026');
    final digest = sha256.convert(bytes);
    return digest.toString();
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter_secure_storage/flutter_secure_storage.dart';
import 'dart:convert';

/// ğŸ”’ Secure Storage Service using flutter_secure_storage
/// Replaces shared_preferences for sensitive data
class SecureStorageService {
  // âœ… FIX: Correct initialization with proper options
  static final SecureStorageService _instance = SecureStorageService._internal();
  factory SecureStorageService() => _instance;
  SecureStorageService._internal();

  static SecureStorageService get instance => _instance;

  // âœ… FIX: Correct initialization with proper options
  final FlutterSecureStorage _storage = const FlutterSecureStorage(
    aOptions: AndroidOptions(
      encryptedSharedPreferences: true,
    ),
  );

  // Storage keys
  static const String _pinKey = 'user_pin';
  static const String _biometricEnabledKey = 'biometric_enabled';
  static const String _businessDataKey = 'business_data';
  static const String _sessionKey = 'session_token';

  /// Save PIN securely
  Future<void> savePin(String pin) async {
    await _storage.write(key: _pinKey, value: pin);
  }

  /// Get saved PIN
  Future<String?> getPin() async {
    return await _storage.read(key: _pinKey);
  }

  /// Check if PIN exists
  Future<bool> hasPinSet() async {
    final pin = await _storage.read(key: _pinKey);
    return pin != null && pin.isNotEmpty;
  }

  /// Save biometric preference
  Future<void> setBiometricEnabled(bool enabled) async {
    await _storage.write(key: _biometricEnabledKey, value: enabled.toString());
  }

  /// Check if biometric is enabled
  Future<bool> isBiometricEnabled() async {
    final value = await _storage.read(key: _biometricEnabledKey);
    return value == 'true';
  }

  /// Save business data
  Future<void> saveBusinessData(Map<String, dynamic> data) async {
    final jsonStr = jsonEncode(data);
    await _storage.write(key: _businessDataKey, value: jsonStr);
  }

  /// Get business data
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>?> getBusinessData() async {
    final jsonStr = await _storage.read(key: _businessDataKey);
    if (jsonStr == null) return null;
    return jsonDecode(jsonStr) as Map<String, dynamic>;
  }

  /// Save session token
  Future<void> saveSessionToken(String token) async {
    await _storage.write(key: _sessionKey, value: token);
  }

  /// Get session token
  Future<String?> getSessionToken() async {
    return await _storage.read(key: _sessionKey);
  }

  /// Get user profile (alias for getBusinessData for compatibility)
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>?> getUserProfile() async {
    return await getBusinessData();
  }

  /// Clear all secure storage (logout)
  Future<void> clearAll() async {
    await _storage.deleteAll();
  }

  /// Clear session only
  Future<void> clearSession() async {
    await _storage.delete(key: _sessionKey);
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'auth_storage_service.dart';
import '../controllers/auth_controller.dart';

/// SESSION MANAGER
/// Handles: App lifecycle, Background/Foreground transitions
class SessionManager extends ChangeNotifier with WidgetsBindingObserver {
  final AuthStorageService _storage;
  final AuthController _authController;
  bool _isLocked = false;

  SessionManager(this._storage, this._authController) {
    WidgetsBinding.instance.addObserver(this);
  }

  @override
  void didChangeAppLifecycleState(AppLifecycleState state) {
    switch (state) {
      case AppLifecycleState.paused:
      case AppLifecycleState.inactive:
      // App going to background - lock session
        _isLocked = true;
        break;

      case AppLifecycleState.resumed:
      // App coming to foreground - check if locked
        if (_isLocked) {
          _handleResumeAuth();
        }
        break;

      default:
        break;
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handleResumeAuth() async {
    if (_storage.isBiometricEnabled) {
      // Trigger biometric authentication
      final success = await _authController.authenticateWithBiometric();
      if (!success) {
        // TODO: Navigate to PIN screen
      }
    } else {
      // TODO: Navigate to PIN screen
    }
    _isLocked = false;
  }

  void dispose() {
    WidgetsBinding.instance.removeObserver(this);
  }
}
```

```dart
/// Validation Service for Invoice Data
class ValidationService {
  /// Validate invoice number uniqueness
  bool validateInvoiceNumber(String invoiceNo, List<String> existingInvoices) {
    return !existingInvoices.contains(invoiceNo.trim());
  }

  /// Validate invoice date (must be within return period)
  bool validateInvoiceDate(DateTime invoiceDate, String month, String year) {
    final returnMonth = _getMonthNumber(month);
    final returnYear = int.parse(year.split('-')[0]);

    return invoiceDate.year == returnYear &&
        invoiceDate.month == returnMonth;
  }

  /// Validate GST rate (0%, 0.25%, 3%, 5%, 12%, 18%, 28%)
  bool validateGSTRate(double rate) {
    const validRates = [0.0, 0.25, 3.0, 5.0, 12.0, 18.0, 28.0];
    return validRates.contains(rate);
  }

  /// Validate tax amount matches taxable value and rate
  bool validateTaxCalculation({
    required double taxableValue,
    required double gstRate,
    required double calculatedTax,
    double tolerance = 1.0, // â‚¹1 tolerance for rounding
  }) {
    final expectedTax = (taxableValue * gstRate) / 100;
    return (expectedTax - calculatedTax).abs() <= tolerance;
  }

  /// Validate customer GSTIN format
  bool validateCustomerGSTIN(String gstin) {
    if (gstin.trim().isEmpty) return true; // B2C allowed
    return RegExp(r'^[0-9]{2}[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z]{1}[1-9A-Z]{1}Z[0-9A-Z]{1}$')
        .hasMatch(gstin);
  }

  /// Validate POS (Place of Supply) matches state code
  bool validatePlaceOfSupply(String pos, String? customerGSTIN) {
    if (customerGSTIN == null || customerGSTIN.isEmpty) return true;
    return pos == customerGSTIN.substring(0, 2);
  }

  /// Check duplicate invoices across multiple Excel files
  List<String> findDuplicateInvoices(List<List<String>> allInvoiceNumbers) {
    final Map<String, int> invoiceCount = {};
    final List<String> duplicates = [];

    for (final invoiceList in allInvoiceNumbers) {
      for (final invoice in invoiceList) {
        invoiceCount[invoice] = (invoiceCount[invoice] ?? 0) + 1;
        if (invoiceCount[invoice]! > 1 && !duplicates.contains(invoice)) {
          duplicates.add(invoice);
        }
      }
    }

    return duplicates;
  }

  int _getMonthNumber(String month) {
    const months = {
      'January': 1, 'February': 2, 'March': 3, 'April': 4,
      'May': 5, 'June': 6, 'July': 7, 'August': 8,
      'September': 9, 'October': 10, 'November': 11, 'December': 12,
    };
    return months[month] ?? 1;
  }
}
```

**Size:** 2.69 KB

```dart
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';

/// Parses cell values from Excel sheets
class ExcelCellParser {
  /// Parse Excel cell value to double - handles all cell types
  static double parseCellValue(Data? cell) {
    if (cell == null || cell.value == null) {
      return 0.0;
    }

    final value = cell.value;

    // âœ… Handle IntCellValue
    if (value is IntCellValue) {
      return value.value.toDouble();
    }

    // âœ… Handle DoubleCellValue
    if (value is DoubleCellValue) {
      return value.value;
    }

    // âœ… Handle TextCellValue (TextSpan â†’ String)
    if (value is TextCellValue) {
      final textSpan = value.value;
      final stringValue = textSpan.toString().trim();

      if (stringValue.isEmpty) {
        return 0.0;
      }

      // Remove currency symbols, commas, spaces
      final cleaned = stringValue
          .replaceAll(RegExp(r'[â‚¹$,\s]'), '')
          .trim();

      return double.tryParse(cleaned) ?? 0.0;
    }

    // âœ… Handle FormulaCellValue (use toString)
    if (value is FormulaCellValue) {
      final stringValue = value.toString().trim();

      if (stringValue.isEmpty) {
        return 0.0;
      }

      final cleaned = stringValue
          .replaceAll(RegExp(r'[â‚¹$,\s]'), '')
          .trim();

      return double.tryParse(cleaned) ?? 0.0;
    }

    // âœ… Fallback: Try to convert to string and parse
    final stringValue = value.toString().trim();
    if (stringValue.isEmpty) {
      return 0.0;
    }

    final cleaned = stringValue
        .replaceAll(RegExp(r'[â‚¹$,\s]'), '')
        .trim();

    return double.tryParse(cleaned) ?? 0.0;
  }

  /// Get cell value as string
  static String? getCellValue(Data? cell) {
    if (cell == null || cell.value == null) return null;

    final value = cell.value;

    // âœ… Handle TextCellValue (TextSpan â†’ String)
    if (value is TextCellValue) {
      return value.value.toString().trim();
    }

    // âœ… Handle IntCellValue
    if (value is IntCellValue) {
      return value.value.toString();
    }

    // âœ… Handle DoubleCellValue
    if (value is DoubleCellValue) {
      return value.value.toString();
    }

    // âœ… Handle FormulaCellValue
    if (value is FormulaCellValue) {
      return value.toString().trim();
    }

    // âœ… Fallback
    return value.toString().trim();
  }

  /// Parse cell value to integer
  static int parseCellValueToInt(Data? cell) {
    final doubleValue = parseCellValue(cell);
    return doubleValue.toInt();
  }

  /// Get numeric value from cell (alias for parseCellValue)
  static double getNumericValue(Data? cell) {
    return parseCellValue(cell);
  }
}

```

```dart
/// Matches date-related columns
class ExcelColumnMatcherDate {
  /// Match order date and return/cancel date columns
  static void matchDateColumns(
      String cellValue,
      int colIndex,
      Map<String, int> tempMap,
      ) {
    // âœ… Order Date - Multiple variations
    if (_isOrderDate(cellValue)) {
      tempMap['orderdate'] = colIndex;
      print('  ğŸ”¹ Found order date at column $colIndex: "$cellValue"');
      return;
    }

    // âœ… Cancel/Return Date
    if (_isCancelReturnDate(cellValue)) {
      tempMap['cancelreturndate'] = colIndex;
      print('  ğŸ”¹ Found cancel/return date at column $colIndex: "$cellValue"');
      return;
    }
  }

  /// Check if cell value matches order date patterns
  static bool _isOrderDate(String cellValue) {
    return (cellValue.contains('order') && cellValue.contains('date')) ||
        cellValue == 'order date' ||
        cellValue == 'orderdate' ||
        cellValue == 'order_date' ||
        cellValue == 'date' ||
        cellValue == 'order dt' ||
        cellValue == 'purchase date' ||
        cellValue == 'sale date';
  }
```

```dart
class ExcelColumnMatcherInfo {

      ) {

      tempMap['invoiceno'] = colIndex;
```

### File 134: excel_data_aggregator.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\excel_data_aggregator.dart`
**Size:** 2.75 KB

```dart
/// Aggregates data by state and HSN code
class ExcelDataAggregator {
  /// Aggregate data by state
  static void aggregateByState({
    required Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> stateWiseData,
    required String state,
    required double taxableValue,
    required double igst,
    required double cgst,
    required double sgst,
    required int quantity,
  }) {
    final stateKey = state.toUpperCase().trim();

    if (!stateWiseData.containsKey(stateKey)) {
      stateWiseData[stateKey] = {
        'taxableValue': 0.0,
        'igst': 0.0,
        'cgst': 0.0,
        'sgst': 0.0,
        'quantity': 0,
      };
    }

    stateWiseData[stateKey]!['taxableValue'] =
        (stateWiseData[stateKey]!['taxableValue'] as double) + taxableValue;
    stateWiseData[stateKey]!['igst'] =
        (stateWiseData[stateKey]!['igst'] as double) + igst;
    stateWiseData[stateKey]!['cgst'] =
        (stateWiseData[stateKey]!['cgst'] as double) + cgst;
    stateWiseData[stateKey]!['sgst'] =
        (stateWiseData[stateKey]!['sgst'] as double) + sgst;
    stateWiseData[stateKey]!['quantity'] =
        (stateWiseData[stateKey]!['quantity'] as int) + quantity;
  }

  /// Aggregate data by HSN code
  static void aggregateByHsn({
    required Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> hsnData,
    required String hsn,
    required int quantity,
    required double taxableValue,
    required double igst,
    required double cgst,
    required double sgst,
  }) {
    if (!hsnData.containsKey(hsn)) {
      hsnData[hsn] = {
        'qty': 0,
        'taxableValue': 0.0,
        'igst': 0.0,
        'cgst': 0.0,
        'sgst': 0.0,
      };
    }

    hsnData[hsn]!['qty'] = (hsnData[hsn]!['qty'] as int) + quantity;
    hsnData[hsn]!['taxableValue'] =
        (hsnData[hsn]!['taxableValue'] as double) + taxableValue;
    hsnData[hsn]!['igst'] = (hsnData[hsn]!['igst'] as double) + igst;
    hsnData[hsn]!['cgst'] = (hsnData[hsn]!['cgst'] as double) + cgst;
    hsnData[hsn]!['sgst'] = (hsnData[hsn]!['sgst'] as double) + sgst;
  }

  /// Calculate totals from state-wise data
  static Map<String, double> calculateTotals(
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> stateWiseData,
      ) {
    double totalTaxable = 0.0;
    double totalIgst = 0.0;
    double totalCgst = 0.0;
    double totalSgst = 0.0;

    stateWiseData.forEach((state, values) {
      totalTaxable += values['taxableValue'] as double;
      totalIgst += values['igst'] as double;
      totalCgst += values['cgst'] as double;
      totalSgst += values['sgst'] as double;
    });

    return {
      'taxable': totalTaxable,
      'igst': totalIgst,
      'cgst': totalCgst,
      'sgst': totalSgst,
      'total': totalIgst + totalCgst + totalSgst,
    };
  }
}
```
