### File 135: excel_date_parser.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\excel_date_parser.dart`
**Size:** 2.31 KB

```dart
import 'excel_constants.dart';

/// Parses date strings in various formats
class ExcelDateParser {
  /// Parse date string to DateTime
  static DateTime? parseDate(String? dateStr) {
    if (dateStr == null || dateStr.trim().isEmpty) return null;

    try {
      // âœ… Format 1: YYYY-MM-DD
      if (dateStr.contains('-') && dateStr.split('-')[0].length == 4) {
        final parts = dateStr.split('-');
        if (parts.length >= 3) {
          return DateTime(
            int.parse(parts[0]),
            int.parse(parts[1]),
            int.parse(parts[2].split(' ')[0]), // Handle "2025-12-15 10:30"
          );
        }
      }

      // âœ… Format 2: DD/MM/YYYY
      if (dateStr.contains('/')) {
        final parts = dateStr.split('/');
        if (parts.length >= 3) {
          return DateTime(
            int.parse(parts[2].split(' ')[0]), // Year
            int.parse(parts[1]), // Month
            int.parse(parts[0]), // Day
          );
        }
      }

      // âœ… Format 3: DD-MM-YYYY
      if (dateStr.contains('-') && dateStr.split('-')[0].length <= 2) {
        final parts = dateStr.split('-');
        if (parts.length >= 3) {
          return DateTime(
            int.parse(parts[2].split(' ')[0]), // Year
            int.parse(parts[1]), // Month
            int.parse(parts[0]), // Day
          );
        }
      }

      // âœ… Format 4: Excel numeric date (e.g., 45292 = 2023-12-01)
      final numericDate = double.tryParse(dateStr);
      if (numericDate != null) {
        // Excel epoch starts from 1899-12-30
        final excelEpoch = DateTime(1899, 12, 30);
        return excelEpoch.add(Duration(days: numericDate.toInt()));
      }
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Date parse error for "$dateStr": $e');
    }

    return null;
  }

  /// Get month name from month number (1-12)
  static String getMonthName(int monthNum) {
    if (monthNum < 1 || monthNum > 12) return '';
    return ExcelConstants.monthNames[monthNum];
  }

  /// Check if date matches selected month
  static bool isDateInMonth(DateTime? date, String selectedMonth) {
    if (date == null) return false;

    final monthName = getMonthName(date.month).toUpperCase();
    final selected = selectedMonth.toUpperCase().trim();

    return monthName == selected;
  }
}

```

### File 136: excel_header_detector.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\excel_header_detector.dart`
**Size:** 2.02 KB

```dart
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
import 'excel_cell_parser.dart';
import 'excel_constants.dart';
import 'excel_column_matcher_date.dart';
import 'excel_column_matcher_financial.dart';
import 'excel_column_matcher_info.dart';
import 'excel_column_matcher_location.dart';

/// Main service to detect header row and map columns
class ExcelHeaderDetector {
  /// Detect header row and return column mapping
  static Map<String, dynamic> detectHeaderRow(Sheet sheet) {
    final columnMap = <String, int>{};

    // Search first 10 rows for header
    for (var i = 0; i < (sheet.rows.length < 10 ? sheet.rows.length : 10); i++) {
      final row = sheet.rows[i];
      if (row.isEmpty) continue;

      final tempMap = <String, int>{};

      // Scan all columns
      for (var colIndex = 0; colIndex < row.length; colIndex++) {
        final cell = row[colIndex];
        if (cell == null || cell.value == null) continue;

        final cellValue = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(cell)?.trim().toLowerCase() ?? '';
        if (cellValue.isEmpty) continue;

        // âœ… Match DATE columns
        ExcelColumnMatcherDate.matchDateColumns(cellValue, colIndex, tempMap);

        // âœ… Match LOCATION columns
        ExcelColumnMatcherLocation.matchLocationColumns(cellValue, colIndex, tempMap);

        // âœ… Match FINANCIAL columns
        ExcelColumnMatcherFinancial.matchFinancialColumns(cellValue, colIndex, tempMap);

        // âœ… Match INFO columns
        ExcelColumnMatcherInfo.matchInfoColumns(cellValue, colIndex, tempMap);
      }

      // If we found enough columns, this is likely the header row
      if (tempMap.length >= ExcelConstants.minColumnsRequired) {
        print('âœ… Valid header row found at $i with ${tempMap.length} columns');
        return {
          'headerRow': i,
          'columnMap': tempMap,
        };
      }
    }

    // No header found
    print('âŒ No valid header row found');
    return {
      'headerRow': 0,
      'columnMap': columnMap,
    };
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'parsers/tax_invoice_parser.dart';
import 'parsers/tcs_sales_parser.dart';
import 'parsers/tcs_return_parser.dart';

/// Main Excel Parser Service
/// Coordinates parsing of all Excel file types
class ExcelParserService {
  // Parser instances
  final TaxInvoiceParser _taxInvoiceParser = TaxInvoiceParser();
  final TcsSalesParser _tcsSalesParser = TcsSalesParser();
  final TcsReturnParser _tcsReturnParser = TcsReturnParser();

  /// Parse Tax Invoice file (Meesho Format)
  /// Filters data by selected month
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parseTaxInvoice(
      String filePath,
      String selectedMonth,
      String selectedYear,
      ) async {
    return await _taxInvoiceParser.parse(filePath, selectedMonth, selectedYear);
  }

  /// Parse TCS Sales file
  /// Filters data by selected month
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parseTcsSales(
      String filePath,
      String selectedMonth,
      String selectedYear,
      ) async {
    return await _tcsSalesParser.parse(filePath, selectedMonth, selectedYear);
  }

  /// Parse TCS Return file (Credit Notes)
  /// Filters data by selected month
  /// Returns return invoice count
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parseTcsReturn(
      String filePath,
      String selectedMonth,
      String selectedYear,
      ) async {
    return await _tcsReturnParser.parse(filePath, selectedMonth, selectedYear);
  }
}
```

### File 138: excel_state_helper.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\excel_state_helper.dart`
**Size:** 875.00 Bytes

```dart
import 'excel_constants.dart';

/// Helper for state-related operations
class ExcelStateHelper {
  /// Get state code from state name
  static String getStateCode(String stateName) {
    return ExcelConstants.stateCodeMap[stateName.toUpperCase().trim()] ?? '99';
  }

  /// Check if transaction is inter-state
  static bool isInterState(String customerState, String supplierStateCode) {
    final stateCode = getStateCode(customerState);
    return stateCode != supplierStateCode;
  }

  /// Validate state name
  static bool isValidState(String? stateName) {
    if (stateName == null || stateName.trim().isEmpty) return false;
    return ExcelConstants.stateCodeMap.containsKey(stateName.toUpperCase().trim());
  }

  /// Normalize state name
  static String normalizeStateName(String stateName) {
    return stateName.toUpperCase().trim();
  }
}
```

### File 139: excel_tax_calculator.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\excel_tax_calculator.dart`
**Size:** 1.23 KB

```dart
import 'excel_state_helper.dart';
import 'excel_constants.dart';

/// Calculates IGST, CGST, SGST based on transaction type
class ExcelTaxCalculator {
  /// Calculate tax breakdown (IGST/CGST/SGST)
  static Map<String, double> calculateTax({
    required String customerState,
    required double taxAmount,
    String? supplierStateCode,
  }) {
    final supplierCode = supplierStateCode ?? ExcelConstants.supplierStateCode;

    final isInterState = ExcelStateHelper.isInterState(customerState, supplierCode);

    if (isInterState) {
      // Inter-state: 100% IGST
      return {
        'igst': taxAmount,
        'cgst': 0.0,
        'sgst': 0.0,
      };
    } else {
      // Intra-state: 50% CGST + 50% SGST
      return {
        'igst': 0.0,
        'cgst': taxAmount / 2,
        'sgst': taxAmount / 2,
      };
    }
  }

  /// Calculate tax from taxable value and rate
  static double calculateTaxFromRate(double taxableValue, double taxRate) {
    return taxableValue * (taxRate / 100);
  }

  /// Get tax rate from tax amount and taxable value
  static double getTaxRate(double taxAmount, double taxableValue) {
    if (taxableValue == 0.0) return 0.0;
    return (taxAmount / taxableValue) * 100;
  }
}

```

### File 140: ExcelDataProcessor.java
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\helpers\ExcelDataProcessor.java`
**Size:** 3.91 KB

```java
import '../excel_constants.dart';
import '../excel_cell_parser.dart';

/// Helper class for processing Excel row data
class ExcelDataProcessor {
  /// Extract data from a row (for Tax Invoice and TCS Sales)
  /// Returns POSITIVE values
  Map<String, dynamic> extractRowData(
    List<Data?> row,
    Map<String, int> columnMap,
  ) {
    // GET STATE
    String state = 'UNKNOWN';
    if (columnMap.containsKey('state')) {
      final stateCell = row[columnMap['state']!];
      if (stateCell != null && stateCell.value != null) {
        state = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(stateCell) ?? 'UNKNOWN';
      }
    }

    // GET TAXABLE VALUE
    double taxable = 0.0;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('taxablevalue')) {
      final cell = row[columnMap['taxablevalue']!];
      if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
        taxable = ExcelCellParser.parseCellValue(cell);
      }
    }

    // GET TAX AMOUNT
    double taxAmount = 0.0;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('taxamount')) {
      final cell = row[columnMap['taxamount']!];
      if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
        taxAmount = ExcelCellParser.parseCellValue(cell);
      }
    }

    // GET HSN CODE
    String hsn = ExcelConstants.defaultHsnCode;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('hsn')) {
      final hsnCell = row[columnMap['hsn']!];
      if (hsnCell != null && hsnCell.value != null) {
        final hsnValue = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(hsnCell);
        if (hsnValue != null && hsnValue.trim().isNotEmpty) {
          hsn = hsnValue.trim();
        }
      }
    }

    // GET QUANTITY
    int qty = 1;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('quantity')) {
      final cell = row[columnMap['quantity']!];
      if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
        qty = ExcelCellParser.parseCellValueToInt(cell);
        if (qty <= 0) qty = 1;
      }
    }

    return {
      'state': state,
      'taxable': taxable,
      'taxAmount': taxAmount,
      'hsn': hsn,
      'qty': qty,
    };
  }

  /// Extract data from a return row (for TCS Return)
  /// Returns NEGATIVE values
  Map<String, dynamic> extractReturnRowData(
    List<Data?> row,
    Map<String, int> columnMap,
  ) {
    // GET STATE
    String state = 'UNKNOWN';
    if (columnMap.containsKey('state')) {
      final stateCell = row[columnMap['state']!];
      if (stateCell != null && stateCell.value != null) {
        state = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(stateCell) ?? 'UNKNOWN';
      }
    }

    // GET TAXABLE VALUE (NEGATIVE)
    double taxable = 0.0;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('taxablevalue')) {
      final cell = row[columnMap['taxablevalue']!];
      if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
        taxable = -ExcelCellParser.parseCellValue(cell); // ğŸ”¥ Negative
      }
    }

    // GET TAX AMOUNT (NEGATIVE)
    double taxAmount = 0.0;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('taxamount')) {
      final cell = row[columnMap['taxamount']!];
      if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
        taxAmount = -ExcelCellParser.parseCellValue(cell); // ğŸ”¥ Negative
      }
    }

    // GET HSN CODE
    String hsn = ExcelConstants.defaultHsnCode;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('hsn')) {
      final hsnCell = row[columnMap['hsn']!];
      if (hsnCell != null && hsnCell.value != null) {
        final hsnValue = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(hsnCell);
        if (hsnValue != null && hsnValue.trim().isNotEmpty) {
          hsn = hsnValue.trim();
        }
      }
    }

    // GET QUANTITY (NEGATIVE)
    int qty = -1;
    if (columnMap.containsKey('quantity')) {
      final cell = row[columnMap['quantity']!];
      if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
        qty = -ExcelCellParser.parseCellValueToInt(cell); // ğŸ”¥ Negative
        if (qty >= 0) qty = -1;
      }
    }

    return {
      'state': state,
      'taxable': taxable,
      'taxAmount': taxAmount,
      'hsn': hsn,
      'qty': qty,
    };
  }
}

```

### File 141: ExcelFileReader.java
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\helpers\ExcelFileReader.java`
**Size:** 448.00 Bytes

```java
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';

/// Helper class for reading Excel files
class ExcelFileReader {
  /// Read and decode Excel file
  Future<Excel> readExcelFile(String filePath) async {
    try {
      final bytes = File(filePath).readAsBytesSync();
      final excel = Excel.decodeBytes(bytes);
      return excel;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error reading Excel file: $e');
      rethrow;
    }
  }
}
```

### File 142: excel_data_processor.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\helpers\excel_data_processor.dart`
**Size:** 2.44 KB

```dart
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
import '../excel_cell_parser.dart';

/// Helper class for processing Excel row data
class ExcelDataProcessor {
  /// Extract row data from Excel row based on column mapping
  Map<String, dynamic> extractRowData(
    List<Data?> row,
    Map<String, int> columnMap,
  ) {
    // State extraction
    String state = 'UNKNOWN';
    for (var stateCol in ['customerstate', 'state', 'placeofsupply', 'pos']) {
      if (columnMap.containsKey(stateCol)) {
        final cell = row[columnMap[stateCol]!];
        if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
          state = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(cell) ?? 'UNKNOWN';
          if (state.isNotEmpty && state != 'UNKNOWN') break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Taxable value extraction
    double taxable = 0.0;
    for (var taxCol in ['taxablevalue', 'taxable', 'taxableamt', 'taxableamount']) {
      if (columnMap.containsKey(taxCol)) {
        final cell = row[columnMap[taxCol]!];
        if (cell != null) {
          taxable = ExcelCellParser.getNumericValue(cell);
          if (taxable != 0.0) break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Tax amount extraction
    double taxAmount = 0.0;
    for (var taxCol in ['taxamount', 'tax', 'totaltax', 'gst', 'gstamount']) {
      if (columnMap.containsKey(taxCol)) {
        final cell = row[columnMap[taxCol]!];
        if (cell != null) {
          taxAmount = ExcelCellParser.getNumericValue(cell);
          if (taxAmount != 0.0) break;
        }
      }
    }

    // HSN code extraction
    String hsn = '8517'; // Default HSN
    for (var hsnCol in ['hsn', 'hsncode', 'hsn_code', 'hsnsac']) {
      if (columnMap.containsKey(hsnCol)) {
        final cell = row[columnMap[hsnCol]!];
        if (cell != null && cell.value != null) {
          hsn = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(cell) ?? '8517';
          if (hsn.isNotEmpty && hsn != '8517') break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Quantity extraction
    int qty = 1;
    for (var qtyCol in ['qty', 'quantity', 'units', 'nos']) {
      if (columnMap.containsKey(qtyCol)) {
        final cell = row[columnMap[qtyCol]!];
        if (cell != null) {
          qty = ExcelCellParser.getNumericValue(cell).toInt();
          if (qty > 0) break;
        }
      }
    }
    if (qty <= 0) qty = 1;

    return {
      'state': state,
      'taxable': taxable,
      'taxAmount': taxAmount,
      'hsn': hsn,
      'qty': qty,
    };
  }
}

```

### File 143: excel_file_reader.dart

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';

/// Helper class for reading Excel files
class ExcelFileReader {
  /// Read Excel file from path
  Future<Excel> readExcelFile(String filePath) async {
    final file = File(filePath);
    final bytes = await file.readAsBytes();
    return Excel.decodeBytes(bytes);
  }
}
```

### File 144: tax_invoice_parser.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\parsers\tax_invoice_parser.dart`
**Size:** 5.93 KB

```dart
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
import '../excel_constants.dart';
import '../excel_header_detector.dart';
import '../excel_cell_parser.dart';
import '../excel_date_parser.dart';
import '../excel_tax_calculator.dart';
import '../excel_data_aggregator.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_file_reader.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_data_processor.dart';

/// Parser for Tax Invoice Excel files
/// Meesho format with order date filtering
class TaxInvoiceParser {
  final ExcelFileReader _fileReader = ExcelFileReader();
  final ExcelDataProcessor _dataProcessor = ExcelDataProcessor();

  /// Parse Tax Invoice file
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parse(
      String filePath,
      String selectedMonth,
      String selectedYear,
      ) async {
    try {
      // Read Excel file
      final excel = await _fileReader.readExcelFile(filePath);

      int count = 0;
      int totalRows = 0;
      int filteredRows = 0;
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> stateWiseData = {};
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> hsnData = {};

      print('ğŸ“‹ Parsing Tax Invoice for $selectedMonth $selectedYear...');

      // Process each sheet
      for (var table in excel.tables.keys) {
        final sheet = excel.tables[table];
        if (sheet == null) continue;

        // Detect header row and column mapping
        final headerInfo = ExcelHeaderDetector.detectHeaderRow(sheet);
        final headerRow = headerInfo['headerRow'] as int;
        final columnMap = headerInfo['columnMap'] as Map<String, int>;

        print('ğŸ“Š Sheet: $table');
        print('   Header at row: $headerRow');
        print('   Columns: ${columnMap.keys.toList()}');

        if (columnMap.isEmpty) {
          print('âš ï¸  No valid columns in sheet $table');
          continue;
        }

        // Process data rows (start from headerRow + 1)
        for (var i = headerRow + 1; i < sheet.rows.length; i++) {
          final row = sheet.rows[i];
          if (row.isEmpty) continue;

          totalRows++;

          try {
            // ===========================
            // 1. GET ORDER DATE
            // ===========================
            String? orderDate;
            if (columnMap.containsKey('orderdate')) {
              final dateCell = row[columnMap['orderdate']!];
              if (dateCell != null && dateCell.value != null) {
                orderDate = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(dateCell);
              }
            }

            // Skip if no order date
            if (orderDate == null || orderDate.trim().isEmpty) {
              if (i < headerRow + 3) {
                print('   Row $i: No order date found');
              }
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            // ===========================
            // 2. FILTER BY MONTH
            // ===========================
            final date = ExcelDateParser.parseDate(orderDate);
            if (date == null) {
              print('   Row $i: Could not parse date: $orderDate');
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            final isMatch = ExcelDateParser.isDateInMonth(date, selectedMonth);
            if (i < headerRow + 3) {
              print('   Row $i: Date=$orderDate | Parsed=${date.toString()} | Month=${date.month} | Match=$isMatch');
            }

            if (!isMatch) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            // ===========================
            // 3. EXTRACT DATA
            // ===========================
            final rowData = _dataProcessor.extractRowData(row, columnMap);

            if (rowData['taxable'] <= 0.0 && rowData['taxAmount'] <= 0.0) {
              if (i < headerRow + 3) {
                print('   Row $i: Zero values - skipped');
              }
              continue;
            }

            // ===========================
            // 4. CALCULATE TAX BREAKDOWN
            // ===========================
            final taxBreakdown = ExcelTaxCalculator.calculateTax(
              customerState: rowData['state'],
              taxAmount: rowData['taxAmount'],
            );

            // ===========================
            // 5. AGGREGATE DATA
            // ===========================
            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByState(
              stateWiseData: stateWiseData,
              state: rowData['state'],
              taxableValue: rowData['taxable'],
              igst: taxBreakdown['igst']!,
              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
            );

            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByHsn(
              hsnData: hsnData,
              hsn: rowData['hsn'],
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
              taxableValue: rowData['taxable'],
              igst: taxBreakdown['igst']!,
              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
            );

            count++;
          } catch (e) {
            print('âŒ Error parsing row $i: $e');
          }
        }
      }

      // Calculate totals
      final totals = ExcelDataAggregator.calculateTotals(stateWiseData);

      print('âœ… Tax Invoice parsed: ${stateWiseData.length} states');
      print('   Total rows: $totalRows');
      print('   Filtered out: $filteredRows');
      print('   Processed: $count invoices');
      print('   Totals: â‚¹${totals['taxable']!.toStringAsFixed(2)} taxable, â‚¹${totals['total']!.toStringAsFixed(2)} tax');

      return {
        'count': count,
        'stateWiseData': stateWiseData,
        'hsnData': hsnData,
      };
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error parsing Tax Invoice: $e');
      return {
        'count': 0,
        'stateWiseData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
        'hsnData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
      };
    }
  }
}

```

### File 145: TcsReturnParser.java
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\parsers\TcsReturnParser.java`
**Size:** 4.45 KB

```java
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
import '../excel_constants.dart';
import '../excel_header_detector.dart';
import '../excel_cell_parser.dart';
import '../excel_date_parser.dart';
import '../excel_tax_calculator.dart';
import '../excel_data_aggregator.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_file_reader.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_data_processor.dart';

/// Parser for TCS Return Excel files (Credit Notes)
/// Returns NEGATIVE values for credit notes
class TcsReturnParser {
  final ExcelFileReader _fileReader = ExcelFileReader();
  final ExcelDataProcessor _dataProcessor = ExcelDataProcessor();

  /// Parse TCS Return file
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parse(
    String filePath,
    String selectedMonth,
    String selectedYear,
  ) async {
    try {
      final excel = await _fileReader.readExcelFile(filePath);

      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> stateWiseData = {};
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> hsnData = {};
      int returnInvoiceCount = 0; // Track credit note count

      print('ğŸ“‹ Parsing TCS Return for $selectedMonth $selectedYear...');

      for (var table in excel.tables.keys) {
        final sheet = excel.tables[table];
        if (sheet == null) continue;

        final headerInfo = ExcelHeaderDetector.detectHeaderRow(sheet);
        final headerRow = headerInfo['headerRow'] as int;
        final columnMap = headerInfo['columnMap'] as Map<String, int>;

        for (var i = headerRow + 1; i < sheet.rows.length; i++) {
          final row = sheet.rows[i];
          if (row.isEmpty) continue;

          try {
            // GET RETURN DATE
            String? returnDate;
            if (columnMap.containsKey('cancelreturndate')) {
              final dateCell = row[columnMap['cancelreturndate']!];
              if (dateCell != null && dateCell.value != null) {
                returnDate = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(dateCell);
              }
            }

            // Filter by month
            if (returnDate != null && returnDate.isNotEmpty) {
              final date = ExcelDateParser.parseDate(returnDate);
              if (date != null && !ExcelDateParser.isDateInMonth(date, selectedMonth)) {
                continue;
              }
            }

            // EXTRACT DATA (as negative values)
            final rowData = _dataProcessor.extractReturnRowData(row, columnMap);
            
            if (rowData['taxable'] >= 0.0 || rowData['taxAmount'] >= 0.0) {
              continue; // Skip positive values
            }

            // ğŸ”¥ INCREMENT RETURN COUNT
            returnInvoiceCount++;

            // CALCULATE TAX
            final taxBreakdown = ExcelTaxCalculator.calculateTax(
              customerState: rowData['state'],
              taxAmount: rowData['taxAmount'],
            );

            // AGGREGATE (values are already negative)
            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByState(
              stateWiseData,
              stateWiseData: stateWiseData,
              state: rowData['state'],
              taxableValue: rowData['taxable'],
              igst: taxBreakdown['igst']!,
              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
            );

            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByHsn(
              hsnData,
              hsnData: hsnData,
              hsn: rowData['hsn'],
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
              taxableValue: rowData['taxable'],
              igst: taxBreakdown['igst']!,
              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
            );
          } catch (e) {
            print('âŒ Error parsing return row $i: $e');
          }
        }
      }

      final totals = ExcelDataAggregator.calculateTotals(stateWiseData);
      print('âœ… TCS Return parsed: ${stateWiseData.length} states');
      print('   Totals: $returnInvoiceCount invoices, â‚¹${totals['taxable']!.toStringAsFixed(2)} taxable, â‚¹${totals['total']!.toStringAsFixed(2)} tax');

      return {
        'returnInvoiceCount': returnInvoiceCount, // ğŸ”¥ Return count
        'stateWiseData': stateWiseData,
        'hsnData': hsnData,
      };
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error parsing TCS Return: $e');
      return {
        'returnInvoiceCount': 0,
        'stateWiseData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
        'hsnData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
      };
    }
  }
}

```

```java
        final columnMap = headerInfo['columnMap'] as Map<String, int>;

        for (var i = headerRow + 1; i < sheet.rows.length; i++) {
          final row = sheet.rows[i];
          if (row.isEmpty) continue;

          try {

              final dateCell = row[columnMap['orderdate']!];

              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
            );

          } catch (e) {
            print('âŒ Error parsing TCS Sales row $i: $e');
          }
        }
      }

      final totals = ExcelDataAggregator.calculateTotals(stateWiseData);
      print('âœ… TCS Sales parsed: ${stateWiseData.length} states, $count invoices');
```

### File 147: tcs_return_parser.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\excel\parsers\tcs_return_parser.dart`
**Size:** 5.33 KB

```dart
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
import '../excel_header_detector.dart';
import '../excel_cell_parser.dart';
import '../excel_date_parser.dart';
import '../excel_tax_calculator.dart';
import '../excel_data_aggregator.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_file_reader.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_data_processor.dart';

/// Parser for TCS Return Excel files (Credit Notes)
/// Handles returns and credit note data
class TcsReturnParser {
  final ExcelFileReader _fileReader = ExcelFileReader();
  final ExcelDataProcessor _dataProcessor = ExcelDataProcessor();

  /// Parse TCS Return file
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parse(
      String filePath,
      String selectedMonth,
      String selectedYear,
      ) async {
    try {
      // Read Excel file
      final excel = await _fileReader.readExcelFile(filePath);

      int count = 0;
      int totalRows = 0;
      int filteredRows = 0;
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> stateWiseData = {};
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> hsnData = {};

      print('ğŸ“‹ Parsing TCS Returns for $selectedMonth $selectedYear...');

      // Process each sheet
      for (var table in excel.tables.keys) {
        final sheet = excel.tables[table];
        if (sheet == null) continue;

        // Detect header row and column mapping
        final headerInfo = ExcelHeaderDetector.detectHeaderRow(sheet);
        final headerRow = headerInfo['headerRow'] as int;
        final columnMap = headerInfo['columnMap'] as Map<String, int>;

        print('ğŸ“Š Sheet: $table');
        print('   Header at row: $headerRow');
        print('   Columns: ${columnMap.keys.toList()}');

        if (columnMap.isEmpty) {
          print('âš ï¸  No valid columns in sheet $table');
          continue;
        }

        // Process data rows (start from headerRow + 1)
        for (var i = headerRow + 1; i < sheet.rows.length; i++) {
          final row = sheet.rows[i];
          if (row.isEmpty) continue;

          totalRows++;

          try {
            // Get date column (try multiple variants)
            String? dateValue;
            for (var dateCol in ['returndate', 'date', 'creditnotedate', 'orderdate']) {
              if (columnMap.containsKey(dateCol)) {
                final dateCell = row[columnMap[dateCol]!];
                if (dateCell != null && dateCell.value != null) {
                  dateValue = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(dateCell);
                  if (dateValue != null && dateValue.isNotEmpty) break;
                }
              }
            }

            // Skip if no date
            if (dateValue == null || dateValue.trim().isEmpty) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            // Filter by month
            final date = ExcelDateParser.parseDate(dateValue);
            if (date == null) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            final isMatch = ExcelDateParser.isDateInMonth(date, selectedMonth);
            if (!isMatch) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            // Extract data
            final rowData = _dataProcessor.extractRowData(row, columnMap);

            // For returns, we expect values (could be positive or negative)
            if (rowData['taxable'] == 0.0 && rowData['taxAmount'] == 0.0) {
              continue;
            }

            // Calculate tax breakdown
            final taxBreakdown = ExcelTaxCalculator.calculateTax(
              customerState: rowData['state'],
              taxAmount: rowData['taxAmount'].abs(), // Use absolute value for calculation
            );

            // Aggregate data (store as negative or absolute based on requirement)
            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByState(
              stateWiseData: stateWiseData,
              state: rowData['state'],
              taxableValue: -rowData['taxable'].abs(), // Store as negative for returns
              igst: -taxBreakdown['igst']!.abs(),
              cgst: -taxBreakdown['cgst']!.abs(),
              sgst: -taxBreakdown['sgst']!.abs(),
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
            );

            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByHsn(
              hsnData: hsnData,
              hsn: rowData['hsn'],
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
              taxableValue: -rowData['taxable'].abs(),
              igst: -taxBreakdown['igst']!.abs(),
              cgst: -taxBreakdown['cgst']!.abs(),
              sgst: -taxBreakdown['sgst']!.abs(),
            );

            count++;
          } catch (e) {
            print('âŒ Error parsing row $i: $e');
          }
        }
      }

      // Calculate totals
      final totals = ExcelDataAggregator.calculateTotals(stateWiseData);

      print('âœ… TCS Returns parsed: ${stateWiseData.length} states');
      print('   Total rows: $totalRows');
      print('   Filtered out: $filteredRows');
      print('   Processed: $count return invoices');

      return {
        'count': count,
        'stateWiseData': stateWiseData,
        'hsnData': hsnData,
      };
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error parsing TCS Returns: $e');
      return {
        'count': 0,
        'stateWiseData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
        'hsnData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
      };
    }
  }
}

```

### File 148: tcs_sales_parser.dart

```dart
import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
import '../excel_header_detector.dart';
import '../excel_cell_parser.dart';
import '../excel_date_parser.dart';
import '../excel_tax_calculator.dart';

import '../helpers/excel_file_reader.dart';
import '../helpers/excel_data_processor.dart';

/// Parser for TCS Sales Excel files
/// Handles TCS sales data with date filtering
class TcsSalesParser {
  final ExcelFileReader _fileReader = ExcelFileReader();
  final ExcelDataProcessor _dataProcessor = ExcelDataProcessor();

  /// Parse TCS Sales file
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parse(
      String filePath,
      String selectedMonth,
      String selectedYear,
      ) async {
    try {
      // Read Excel file
      final excel = await _fileReader.readExcelFile(filePath);

      int count = 0;
      int totalRows = 0;
      int filteredRows = 0;
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> stateWiseData = {};
      Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>> hsnData = {};

      print('ğŸ“‹ Parsing TCS Sales for $selectedMonth $selectedYear...');

      // Process each sheet
      for (var table in excel.tables.keys) {
        final sheet = excel.tables[table];
        if (sheet == null) continue;

        // Detect header row and column mapping
        final headerInfo = ExcelHeaderDetector.detectHeaderRow(sheet);
        final headerRow = headerInfo['headerRow'] as int;
        final columnMap = headerInfo['columnMap'] as Map<String, int>;

        print('ğŸ“Š Sheet: $table');
        print('   Header at row: $headerRow');
        print('   Columns: ${columnMap.keys.toList()}');

        if (columnMap.isEmpty) {
          print('âš ï¸  No valid columns in sheet $table');
          continue;
        }

        // Process data rows (start from headerRow + 1)
        for (var i = headerRow + 1; i < sheet.rows.length; i++) {
          final row = sheet.rows[i];
          if (row.isEmpty) continue;

          totalRows++;

          try {
            // Get date column (try multiple variants)
            String? dateValue;
            for (var dateCol in ['orderdate', 'date', 'invoicedate', 'saledate']) {
              if (columnMap.containsKey(dateCol)) {
                final dateCell = row[columnMap[dateCol]!];
                if (dateCell != null && dateCell.value != null) {
                  dateValue = ExcelCellParser.getCellValue(dateCell);
                  if (dateValue != null && dateValue.isNotEmpty) break;
                }
              }
            }

            // Skip if no date
            if (dateValue == null || dateValue.trim().isEmpty) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            // Filter by month
            final date = ExcelDateParser.parseDate(dateValue);
            if (date == null) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            final isMatch = ExcelDateParser.isDateInMonth(date, selectedMonth);
            if (!isMatch) {
              filteredRows++;
              continue;
            }

            // Extract data
            final rowData = _dataProcessor.extractRowData(row, columnMap);

            if (rowData['taxable'] <= 0.0 && rowData['taxAmount'] <= 0.0) {
              continue;
            }

            // Calculate tax breakdown
            final taxBreakdown = ExcelTaxCalculator.calculateTax(
              customerState: rowData['state'],
              taxAmount: rowData['taxAmount'],
            );

            // Aggregate data
            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByState(
              stateWiseData: stateWiseData,
              state: rowData['state'],
              taxableValue: rowData['taxable'],
              igst: taxBreakdown['igst']!,
              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
            );

            ExcelDataAggregator.aggregateByHsn(
              hsnData: hsnData,
              hsn: rowData['hsn'],
              quantity: rowData['qty'],
              taxableValue: rowData['taxable'],
              igst: taxBreakdown['igst']!,
              cgst: taxBreakdown['cgst']!,
              sgst: taxBreakdown['sgst']!,
            );

            count++;
          } catch (e) {
            print('âŒ Error parsing row $i: $e');
          }
        }
      }

      // Calculate totals
      final totals = ExcelDataAggregator.calculateTotals(stateWiseData);

      print('âœ… TCS Sales parsed: ${stateWiseData.length} states');
      print('   Total rows: $totalRows');
      print('   Filtered out: $filteredRows');
      print('   Processed: $count invoices');

      return {
        'count': count,
        'stateWiseData': stateWiseData,
        'hsnData': hsnData,
      };
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error parsing TCS Sales: $e');
      return {
        'count': 0,
        'stateWiseData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
        'hsnData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
      };
    }
  }
}
```

### File 149: filing_data_processor.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\filing\filing_data_processor.dart`
**Size:** 4.75 KB

```dart
import '../../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../excel/excel_parser_service.dart';

/// Handles Excel parsing and data merging operations
class FilingDataProcessor {
  final ExcelParserService _excelParser = ExcelParserService();

  /// Parse Excel file based on type
  Future<Map<String, dynamic>> parseFile({
    required String fileType,
    required String filePath,
    required String month,
    required String year,
  }) async {
    Map<String, dynamic> processedData;

    if (fileType == 'taxinvoice') {
      processedData = await _excelParser.parseTaxInvoice(
        filePath,
        month,
        year,
      );
    } else if (fileType == 'tcssales') {
      processedData = await _excelParser.parseTcsSales(
        filePath,
        month,
        year,
      );
    } else if (fileType == 'tcsreturn') {
      processedData = await _excelParser.parseTcsReturn(
        filePath,
        month,
        year,
      );
    } else {
      processedData = {
        'count': 0,
        'stateWiseData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
        'hsnData': <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{},
      };
    }

    return processedData;
  }

  /// Merge new data with existing filing data
  Map<String, dynamic> mergeData(
      FilingData currentData,
      Map<String, dynamic> newData,
      ) {
    final merged = <String, dynamic>{};

    // ===========================
    // MERGE STATE-WISE DATA
    // ===========================
    final mergedStateData = <String, Map<String, dynamic>>{};

    // Add existing data
    if (currentData.stateWiseData != null) {
      currentData.stateWiseData!.forEach((state, values) {
        mergedStateData[state] = Map<String, dynamic>.from(values);
      });
    }

    // Add new data
    if (newData['stateWiseData'] != null) {
      (newData['stateWiseData'] as Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>>)
          .forEach((state, values) {
        if (!mergedStateData.containsKey(state)) {
          // Create new state entry
          mergedStateData[state] = {
            'taxableValue': 0.0,
            'igst': 0.0,
            'cgst': 0.0,
            'sgst': 0.0,
            'quantity': 0,
          };
        }

        // Merge values
        mergedStateData[state]!['taxableValue'] =
            (mergedStateData[state]!['taxableValue'] as double) +
                (values['taxableValue'] as double);
        mergedStateData[state]!['igst'] =
            (mergedStateData[state]!['igst'] as double) +
                (values['igst'] as double);
        mergedStateData[state]!['cgst'] =
            (mergedStateData[state]!['cgst'] as double) +
                (values['cgst'] as double);
        mergedStateData[state]!['sgst'] =
            (mergedStateData[state]!['sgst'] as double) +
                (values['sgst'] as double);
        mergedStateData[state]!['quantity'] =
            (mergedStateData[state]!['quantity'] as int) +
                (values['quantity'] as int);
      });
    }

    // ===========================
    // COUNT INVOICES
    // ===========================
    int totalCount = currentData.totalInvoices;
    if (newData['count'] != null) {
      totalCount += newData['count'] as int;
    }

    // ===========================
    // COUNT RETURN INVOICES
    // ===========================
    int totalReturnInvoices = currentData.returnInvoices;
    if (newData['returnInvoiceCount'] != null) {
      totalReturnInvoices += newData['returnInvoiceCount'] as int;
    }

    merged['stateWiseData'] = mergedStateData;
    merged['count'] = totalCount;
    merged['returnInvoices'] = totalReturnInvoices;

    return merged;
  }

  /// Calculate totals from state-wise data
  Map<String, dynamic> calculateTotals(Map<String, dynamic> mergedData) {
    double totalTaxable = 0.0;
    double totalIgst = 0.0;
    double totalCgst = 0.0;
    double totalSgst = 0.0;

    // Sum up all state-wise values
    if (mergedData['stateWiseData'] != null) {
      (mergedData['stateWiseData'] as Map<String, Map<String, dynamic>>)
          .forEach((state, values) {
        totalTaxable += values['taxableValue'] as double;
        totalIgst += values['igst'] as double;
        totalCgst += values['cgst'] as double;
        totalSgst += values['sgst'] as double;
      });
    }

    final totalTax = totalIgst + totalCgst + totalSgst;
    final invoiceCount = mergedData['count'] ?? 0;
    final returnInvoices = mergedData['returnInvoices'] ?? 0;

    return {
      'totalTaxable': totalTaxable,
      'totalIgst': totalIgst,
      'totalCgst': totalCgst,
      'totalSgst': totalSgst,
      'totalTax': totalTax,
      'invoiceCount': invoiceCount,
      'returnInvoices': returnInvoices,
    };
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:file_picker/file_picker.dart';
import '../../models/uploaded_file.dart';

/// Handles file picking and upload status management
class FilingFileHandler {
  /// Pick Excel file from device
  Future<String?> pickFile() async {
    try {
      final result = await FilePicker.platform.pickFiles(
        type: FileType.custom,
        allowedExtensions: ['xlsx', 'xls'],
      );

      return result?.files.single.path;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error picking file: $e');
      return null;
    }
  }

  /// Update file upload status in the list
  List<UploadedFile> updateFileStatus(
      List<UploadedFile> files,
      String fileType,
      String filePath,
      ) {
    return files.map((file) {
      if (file.id == fileType) {
        return file.copyWith(
          isUploaded: true,
          filePath: filePath,
          uploadedAt: DateTime.now(),
        );
      }
      return file;
    }).toList();
  }
}
```

### File 152: json_generator_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\json\json_generator_service.dart`
**Size:** 9.33 KB

```dart
import 'dart:convert';
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import '../../models/filing_data.dart';

class JsonGeneratorService {

  /// Main function to generate GSTR-1 JSON
  String generateJson(FilingData data) {
    // Build the JSON Structure using state-wise data
    final Map<String, dynamic> jsonMap = {
      "gstin": data.gstin.trim().toUpperCase(),
      "fp": _getFinancialPeriod(data.month, data.year),
      "gt": data.taxableValue + data.totalTax,
      "cur_gt": data.taxableValue + data.totalTax,
      "version": "GST3.1.9",
      "hash": "hash",

      // Sections
      "b2cs": _generateB2CsSection(data),
      "cdnur": _generateCdnurSection(data),
      "hsn": _generateHsnSection(data),
    };

    // Sanitize (Remove trailing spaces recursively)
    final sanitizedMap = _sanitizeJson(jsonMap);

    return jsonEncode(sanitizedMap);
  }

  /// Generate and download JSON file
  Future<String?> generateAndDownload(FilingData data) async {
    try {
      final jsonString = generateJson(data);
      
      // Get the downloads directory
      final directory = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
      final fileName = 'GSTR1_${data.gstin}_${data.month}_${data.year}.json';
      final filePath = '${directory.path}/$fileName';
      
      // Write to file
      final file = File(filePath);
      await file.writeAsString(jsonString);
      
      print('âœ… JSON saved to: $filePath');
      return filePath;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error generating JSON: $e');
      return null;
    }
  }

  /// Generates Financial Period in MMYYYY format
  String _getFinancialPeriod(String month, String year) {
    String monthNum = _getMonthNumber(month);
    return "$monthNum$year";
  }

  String _getMonthNumber(String monthName) {
    switch (monthName.toLowerCase().trim()) {
      case 'january': case 'jan': return '01';
      case 'february': case 'feb': return '02';
      case 'march': case 'mar': return '03';
      case 'april': case 'apr': return '04';
      case 'may': return '05';
      case 'june': case 'jun': return '06';
      case 'july': case 'jul': return '07';
      case 'august': case 'aug': return '08';
      case 'september': case 'sep': return '09';
      case 'october': case 'oct': return '10';
      case 'november': case 'nov': return '11';
      case 'december': case 'dec': return '12';
      default: return monthName.padLeft(2, '0');
    }
  }

  /// Generates B2CS Section from state-wise data (Positive Sales)
  List<Map<String, dynamic>> _generateB2CsSection(FilingData data) {
    if (data.stateWiseData == null || data.stateWiseData!.isEmpty) return [];

    List<Map<String, dynamic>> b2csList = [];

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((state, stateData) {
      double taxable = (stateData['taxable'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      double igst = (stateData['igst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      double cgst = (stateData['cgst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      double sgst = (stateData['sgst'] ?? 0.0) as double;

      // Only include positive values in B2CS
      if (taxable > 0) {
        // Determine supply type based on IGST vs CGST/SGST
        String supplyType = igst > 0 ? "INTER" : "INTRA";
        String pos = _getStateCode(state);
        
        // Calculate rate (assuming standard rate, can be refined)
        double taxAmount = igst > 0 ? igst : (cgst + sgst);
        double rate = taxable > 0 ? (taxAmount / taxable * 100) : 0.0;
        rate = _roundToNearestRate(rate);

        b2csList.add({
          "sply_ty": supplyType,
          "txval": _round(taxable),
          "pos": pos,
          "typ": "OE",
          "rt": rate,
          "iamt": _round(igst),
          "camt": _round(cgst),
          "samt": _round(sgst),
          "csamt": 0.0
        });
      }
    });

    return b2csList;
  }

  /// Generates CDNUR Section (For Returns/Negative Values)
  List<Map<String, dynamic>> _generateCdnurSection(FilingData data) {
    if (data.stateWiseData == null || data.stateWiseData!.isEmpty) return [];
    if (data.returnInvoices == 0) return [];

    List<Map<String, dynamic>> cdnurList = [];

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((state, stateData) {
      double taxable = (stateData['taxable'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      double igst = (stateData['igst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      double cgst = (stateData['cgst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      double sgst = (stateData['sgst'] ?? 0.0) as double;

      // Only include negative values (returns) in CDNUR
      if (taxable < 0) {
        String supplyType = igst.abs() > 0 ? "INTER" : "INTRA";
        String pos = _getStateCode(state);
        
        double taxAmount = igst.abs() > 0 ? igst.abs() : (cgst.abs() + sgst.abs());
        double rate = taxable.abs() > 0 ? (taxAmount / taxable.abs() * 100) : 0.0;
        rate = _roundToNearestRate(rate);

        double totalVal = taxable.abs() + igst.abs() + cgst.abs() + sgst.abs();

        cdnurList.add({
          "typ": "OE",
          "ntty": "C",
          "sply_ty": supplyType,
          "p_gst": "N",
          "inum": "CDN-${DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch}",
          "idt": "01-${DateTime.now().month.toString().padLeft(2,'0')}-${DateTime.now().year}",
          "val": _round(totalVal),
          "pos": pos,
          "itms": [
            {
              "num": 1,
              "itm_det": {
                "rt": rate,
                "txval": _round(taxable.abs()),
                "iamt": _round(igst.abs()),
                "camt": _round(cgst.abs()),
                "samt": _round(sgst.abs()),
                "csamt": 0.0
              }
            }
          ]
        });
      }
    });

    return cdnurList;
  }

  /// Generates HSN Section from state-wise data
  Map<String, dynamic> _generateHsnSection(FilingData data) {
    if (data.stateWiseData == null || data.stateWiseData!.isEmpty) {
      return {"data": []};
    }

    // Aggregate all positive (sales) data for HSN
    double totalQty = 0.0;
    double totalTaxable = 0.0;
    double totalIgst = 0.0;
    double totalCgst = 0.0;
    double totalSgst = 0.0;

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((state, stateData) {
      double taxable = (stateData['taxable'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      if (taxable > 0) {
        totalQty += (stateData['quantity'] ?? 1.0) as double;
        totalTaxable += taxable;
        totalIgst += (stateData['igst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
        totalCgst += (stateData['cgst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
        totalSgst += (stateData['sgst'] ?? 0.0) as double;
      }
    });

    if (totalTaxable == 0) return {"data": []};

    double totalVal = totalTaxable + totalIgst + totalCgst + totalSgst;

    List<Map<String, dynamic>> hsnList = [
      {
        "num": 1,
        "hsn_sc": "8517",
        "desc": "Goods",
        "uqc": "NOS",
        "qty": _round(totalQty),
        "val": _round(totalVal),
        "txval": _round(totalTaxable),
        "iamt": _round(totalIgst),
        "camt": _round(totalCgst),
        "samt": _round(totalSgst),
        "csamt": 0.0
      }
    ];

    return {"data": hsnList};
  }

  /// Get state code from state name
  String _getStateCode(String stateName) {
    const stateCodeMap = {
      'andhra pradesh': '37',
      'arunachal pradesh': '12',
      'assam': '18',
      'bihar': '10',
      'chhattisgarh': '22',
      'goa': '30',
      'gujarat': '24',
      'haryana': '06',
      'himachal pradesh': '02',
      'jharkhand': '20',
      'karnataka': '29',
      'kerala': '32',
      'madhya pradesh': '23',
      'maharashtra': '27',
      'manipur': '14',
      'meghalaya': '17',
      'mizoram': '15',
      'nagaland': '13',
      'odisha': '21',
      'punjab': '03',
      'rajasthan': '08',
      'sikkim': '11',
      'tamil nadu': '33',
      'telangana': '36',
      'tripura': '16',
      'uttar pradesh': '09',
      'uttarakhand': '05',
      'west bengal': '19',
      'delhi': '07',
      'jammu and kashmir': '01',
      'ladakh': '38',
      'chandigarh': '04',
      'puducherry': '34',
      'andaman and nicobar': '35',
      'dadra and nagar haveli': '26',
      'daman and diu': '25',
      'lakshadweep': '31',
    };
    
    return stateCodeMap[stateName.toLowerCase().trim()] ?? '00';
  }

  /// Round rate to nearest standard GST rate
  double _roundToNearestRate(double rate) {
    const standardRates = [0, 5, 12, 18, 28];
    double closest = standardRates[0].toDouble();
    double minDiff = (rate - closest).abs();
    
    for (var stdRate in standardRates) {
      double diff = (rate - stdRate).abs();
      if (diff < minDiff) {
        minDiff = diff;
        closest = stdRate.toDouble();
      }
    }
    return closest;
  }

  /// Helper to round double to 2 decimal places
  double _round(double val) {
    return double.parse(val.toStringAsFixed(2));
  }

  /// Recursive function to remove trailing spaces from Strings in JSON
  dynamic _sanitizeJson(dynamic data) {
    if (data is String) {
      return data.trim();
    } else if (data is Map) {
      Map<String, dynamic> newMap = {};
      data.forEach((key, value) {
        newMap[key.trim()] = _sanitizeJson(value);
      });
      return newMap;
    } else if (data is List) {
      return data.map((e) => _sanitizeJson(e)).toList();
    }
    return data;
  }
}
```

### File 153: b2cs_generator.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\json\generators\b2cs_generator.dart`
**Size:** 1.97 KB

```dart
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../helpers/json_helpers.dart';

/// B2CS Section Generator
/// GST Tool Format: Only POSITIVE values (sales)
/// Negative values go to CDNUR
class B2CSGenerator {
  /// Generate B2CS section
  /// Rule: Only positive taxable values
  List<Map<String, dynamic>> generate(FilingData data) {
    final b2csList = <Map<String, dynamic>>[];

    if (data.stateWiseData == null) return b2csList;

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((stateName, values) {
      final stateCode = JsonHelpers.getStateCode(stateName);
      final isInterState = stateCode != '10'; // Supplier in Bihar (10)

      final taxable = values['taxableValue'] as double;
      final igst = values['igst'] as double;
      final cgst = values['cgst'] as double;
      final sgst = values['sgst'] as double;

      // ğŸ”¥ CRITICAL: Skip negative values (returns go to CDNUR)
      if (taxable <= 0.0) return;

      // INTRA validation: Only Bihar (10) can be INTRA
      String supplyType;
      if (isInterState) {
        supplyType = 'INTER';
      } else {
        // Double-check INTRA only for home state
        if (stateCode != '10') {
          print('âš ï¸ Warning: State $stateName (code $stateCode) should be INTER, not INTRA');
          supplyType = 'INTER'; // Force INTER if not Bihar
        } else {
          supplyType = 'INTRA';
        }
      }

      final entry = <String, dynamic>{
        'splyty': supplyType,
        'rt': 5, // 5% GST rate
        'typ': 'OE', // E-commerce
        'pos': stateCode,
        'txval': JsonHelpers.round(taxable),
        'csamt': 0,
      };

      if (isInterState) {
        entry['iamt'] = JsonHelpers.round(igst);
      } else {
        entry['camt'] = JsonHelpers.round(cgst);
        entry['samt'] = JsonHelpers.round(sgst);
      }

      b2csList.add(entry);
    });

    print('ğŸ“Š B2CS: ${b2csList.length} state entries (positive only)');
    return b2csList;
  }
}

```

```dart
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../helpers/json_helpers.dart';

/// CDNUR Section Generator
/// GST Tool Format: Credit Notes for unregistered customers
/// Contains negative values as POSITIVE (absolute)
class CDNURGenerator {
  /// Generate CDNUR section
  /// Rule: Only negative taxable values (returns/credit notes)
  List<Map<String, dynamic>> generate(FilingData data) {
    final cdnurList = <Map<String, dynamic>>[];

    if (data.stateWiseData == null) return cdnurList;

    int creditNoteCounter = 838; // Starting credit note number
    final year = data.year.trim().substring(2, 4); // '26' from '2026'

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((stateName, values) {
      final stateCode = JsonHelpers.getStateCode(stateName);
      final isInterState = stateCode != '10';

      final taxable = values['taxableValue'] as double;
      final igst = values['igst'] as double;
      final cgst = values['cgst'] as double;
      final sgst = values['sgst'] as double;

      // ğŸ”¥ Only negative values (credit notes)
      if (taxable >= 0.0) return;

      // Complete CDNUR structure with all mandatory fields
      final entry = <String, dynamic>{
        'ntty': 'C', // Credit Note
        'ntnum': 'EST${year}C$creditNoteCounter', // Credit note number
        'ntdt': JsonHelpers.getFormattedDate(data.month, data.year), // Credit note date
        'inum': 'EST${year}${1078 + (creditNoteCounter - 839)}', // Original invoice ref
        'idt': JsonHelpers.getFormattedDate(data.month, data.year), // Original invoice date
        'typ': 'OE', // E-commerce
        'pos': stateCode,
        'val': JsonHelpers.round(taxable.abs()), // Absolute value with rounding
        'rt': 5,
      };

      if (isInterState) {
        entry['iamt'] = JsonHelpers.round(igst.abs());
      } else {
        entry['camt'] = JsonHelpers.round(cgst.abs());
        entry['samt'] = JsonHelpers.round(sgst.abs());
      }

      cdnurList.add(entry);
      creditNoteCounter++;
    });

    print('ğŸ“ CDNUR: ${cdnurList.length} credit note entries (complete structure)');
    return cdnurList;
  }
}
```

```dart
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';

/// DOCISSUE Section Generator
/// GST Tool Format: Invoice and credit note ranges
class DOCISSUEGenerator {
  /// Generate DOCISSUE section
  /// Rule: Invoice ranges from Excel data
  Map<String, dynamic> generate(FilingData data) {
    final docDet = <Map<String, dynamic>>[];

    // Invoice range
    if (data.totalInvoices > 0) {
      // ğŸ”¥ FIXED: Invoice format EST261078 (not estru)
      final yearCode = data.year.trim().substring(2, 4);
      final invoiceFrom = 'EST${yearCode}1078';
      final invoiceTo = 'EST$yearCode${1078 + data.totalInvoices - 1}';

      docDet.add({
        'docnum': 1,
        'doctyp': 'Invoices for outward supply',
        'docs': [
          {
            'num': 1,
            'from': invoiceFrom,
            'to': invoiceTo,
            'totnum': data.totalInvoices,
            'cancel': 0,
            'netissue': data.totalInvoices,
          }
        ],
      });
    }

    // Credit Note range
    // ğŸ”¥ FIXED: Use actual invoice count from returns data
    int creditNoteCount = data.returnInvoices;

    if (creditNoteCount > 0) {
      final yearCode = data.year.trim().substring(2, 4);
      final creditFrom = 'EST${yearCode}C838';
      final creditTo = 'EST${yearCode}C${838 + creditNoteCount - 1}';

      docDet.add({
        'docnum': 5,
        'doctyp': 'Credit Note',
        'docs': [
          {
            'num': 1,
            'from': creditFrom,
            'to': creditTo,
            'totnum': creditNoteCount,
            'cancel': 0,
            'netissue': creditNoteCount,
          }
        ],
      });
    }

    print('ğŸ“‹ DOCISSUE: ${docDet.length} document types');
    return {'docdet': docDet};
  }
}
```

### File 156: hsn_generator.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\json\generators\hsn_generator.dart`
**Size:** 2.57 KB

```dart
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../helpers/json_helpers.dart';

/// HSN Section Generator
/// GST Tool Format: Separate INTER and INTRA rows
/// Only B2CS data (positive values), CDNUR excluded
class HSNGenerator {
  /// Generate HSN section
  /// Rule: B2CS sum only, INTER/INTRA split
  Map<String, dynamic> generate(FilingData data) {
    final hsnList = <Map<String, dynamic>>[];

    if (data.stateWiseData == null) {
      return {'hsnb2c': hsnList};
    }

    // Separate tracking for INTER-state and INTRA-state
    double interTaxable = 0.0;
    double interIgst = 0.0;
    int interQty = 0;

    double intraTaxable = 0.0;
    double intraCgst = 0.0;
    double intraSgst = 0.0;
    int intraQty = 0;

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((stateName, values) {
      final taxable = values['taxableValue'] as double;
      final qty = values['quantity'] as int;

      // ğŸ”¥ CRITICAL: Only positive values (B2CS only, CDNUR excluded)
      if (taxable <= 0.0) return;

      final stateCode = JsonHelpers.getStateCode(stateName);
      final isInterState = stateCode != '10'; // Bihar = 10

      if (isInterState) {
        // INTER-state: IGST
        interTaxable += taxable;
        interIgst += values['igst'] as double;
        interQty += qty;
      } else {
        // INTRA-state: CGST + SGST
        intraTaxable += taxable;
        intraCgst += values['cgst'] as double;
        intraSgst += values['sgst'] as double;
        intraQty += qty;
      }
    });

    int rowNum = 1;

    // Add INTER-state HSN row (if exists)
    if (interTaxable > 0.0) {
      hsnList.add({
        'num': rowNum++,
        'hsnsc': '610990',
        'uqc': 'PCS',
        'qty': interQty,
        'rt': 5,
        'txval': JsonHelpers.round(interTaxable),
        'iamt': JsonHelpers.round(interIgst), // Only IGST
        'camt': 0.0, // No CGST
        'samt': 0.0, // No SGST
        'csamt': 0,
      });
    }

    // Add INTRA-state HSN row (if exists)
    if (intraTaxable > 0.0) {
      hsnList.add({
        'num': rowNum,
        'hsnsc': '610990',
        'uqc': 'PCS',
        'qty': intraQty,
        'rt': 5,
        'txval': JsonHelpers.round(intraTaxable),
        'iamt': 0.0, // No IGST
        'camt': JsonHelpers.round(intraCgst), // CGST
        'samt': JsonHelpers.round(intraSgst), // SGST
        'csamt': 0,
      });
    }

    print('ğŸ“¦ HSN: ${hsnList.length} entries (INTER: ${interTaxable > 0 ? 'âœ“' : ''}, INTRA: ${intraTaxable > 0 ? 'âœ“' : ''})');
    return {'hsnb2c': hsnList};
  }
}
```

```dart
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';
import '../helpers/json_helpers.dart';

/// SUPECO Section Generator
/// GST Tool Format: E-commerce operator data
/// NET values (B2CS - CDNUR)
class SUPECOGenerator {
  /// Generate SUPECO section
  /// Rule: Only for E-commerce operators
  Map<String, dynamic> generate(FilingData data) {
    if (data.stateWiseData == null) {
      return {'clttx': []};
    }

    // Aggregate all values (NET including returns)
    double totalSupply = 0.0;
    double totalIgst = 0.0;
    double totalCgst = 0.0;
    double totalSgst = 0.0;

    data.stateWiseData!.forEach((state, values) {
      totalSupply += values['taxableValue'] as double;
      totalIgst += values['igst'] as double;
      totalCgst += values['cgst'] as double;
      totalSgst += values['sgst'] as double;
    });

    final clttx = <Map<String, dynamic>>[];

    if (totalSupply != 0.0) {
      clttx.add({
        'etin': '10AARCM9332R1C3', // Meesho GSTIN
        'suppval': JsonHelpers.round(totalSupply),
        'igst': JsonHelpers.round(totalIgst),
        'cgst': JsonHelpers.round(totalCgst),
        'sgst': JsonHelpers.round(totalSgst),
        'cess': 0,
        'flag': 'N',
      });
      print('ğŸ¢ SUPECO: Meesho platform entry');
    }

    return {'clttx': clttx};
  }
}
```

### File 158: json_file_manager.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\json\helpers\json_file_manager.dart`
**Size:** 1.12 KB

```dart
import 'dart:convert';
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import '../../../models/filing_data.dart';
import 'json_helpers.dart';

/// JSON File Manager
/// Handles saving JSON files to device
class JsonFileManager {
  /// Save JSON file to M-GST/Returns folder
  Future<String?> saveJsonFile(
      Map<String, dynamic> jsonData,
      FilingData data,
      ) async {
    try {
      final directory = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
      final returnsDir = Directory('${directory.path}/M-GST/Returns');

      if (!await returnsDir.exists()) {
        await returnsDir.create(recursive: true);
      }

      final fileName =
          'GSTR1_returns_${data.gstin}_monthly_${JsonHelpers.getFinancialPeriod(data.month, data.year)}.json';
      final file = File('${returnsDir.path}/$fileName');

      // Convert to pretty JSON
      final jsonString = const JsonEncoder.withIndent('  ').convert(jsonData);
      await file.writeAsString(jsonString);

      return file.path;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error saving file: $e');
      return null;
    }
  }
}
```

### File 159: json_helpers.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\json\helpers\json_helpers.dart`
**Size:** 2.74 KB

```dart
/// JSON Helper Functions
/// Utility functions for JSON generation
class JsonHelpers {
  /// Round to 2 decimal places
  static double round(double value) {
    return double.parse(value.toStringAsFixed(2));
  }

  /// Sanitize JSON - Remove trailing spaces recursively
  static dynamic sanitizeJson(dynamic value) {
    if (value is String) {
      return value.trim(); // Remove ALL leading/trailing spaces
    } else if (value is Map) {
      // Cast to Map<String, dynamic>
      return value.map((k, v) => MapEntry(
        k is String ? k.trim() : k, // Sanitize keys
        sanitizeJson(v), // Sanitize values recursively
      )).cast<String, dynamic>();
    } else if (value is List) {
      return value.map((item) => sanitizeJson(item)).toList();
    }
    return value; // Numbers, bools, null stay as-is
  }

  /// Get financial period (MMYYYY format)
  static String getFinancialPeriod(String month, String year) {
    final monthNum = getMonthNumber(month.trim()); // Trim month
    final yearNum = year.trim().split('-')[0]; // '2025-26' -> '2025'
    return '${monthNum.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}$yearNum';
  }

  /// Get month number (1-12)
  static int getMonthNumber(String month) {
    const months = {
      'JANUARY': 1,
      'FEBRUARY': 2,
      'MARCH': 3,
      'APRIL': 4,
      'MAY': 5,
      'JUNE': 6,
      'JULY': 7,
      'AUGUST': 8,
      'SEPTEMBER': 9,
      'OCTOBER': 10,
      'NOVEMBER': 11,
      'DECEMBER': 12,
    };
    return months[month.trim().toUpperCase()] ?? 1; // Trim before lookup
  }

  /// Get formatted date (DDMMYYYY) for CDNUR
  static String getFormattedDate(String month, String year) {
    final monthNum = getMonthNumber(month);
    final yearNum = year.trim().split('-')[0]; // '2025-26' -> '2025'

    // Get last day of month
    final lastDay = DateTime(int.parse(yearNum), monthNum + 1, 0).day;

    return '${lastDay.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}${monthNum.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}$yearNum';
  }

  /// Get state code from state name
  static String getStateCode(String stateName) {
    const stateCodeMap = {
      'ANDHRA PRADESH': '37',
      'BIHAR': '10',
      'GUJARAT': '24',
      'HARYANA': '06',
      'JHARKHAND': '20',
      'KARNATAKA': '29',
      'MAHARASHTRA': '27',
      'ORISSA': '21',
      'ODISHA': '21',
      'RAJASTHAN': '08',
      'TAMIL NADU': '33',
      'TELANGANA': '36',
      'UTTAR PRADESH': '09',
      'WEST BENGAL': '19',
      'ASSAM': '18',
    };

    final code = stateCodeMap[stateName.toUpperCase().trim()];
    if (code == null) {
      print('âš ï¸ Unknown state: $stateName - using state code from data');
      return '18'; // Default to Assam if state unknown
    }
    return code;
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../constants/dashboard_strings.dart';

class BottomNavBar extends StatelessWidget {
  final int currentIndex;
  final Function(int) onTap;

  const BottomNavBar({
    super.key,
    required this.currentIndex,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        border: Border(
          top: BorderSide(color: AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5), width: 1),
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8),
          child: Row(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
            children: [
              _buildNavItem(
                icon: Icons.home,
                label: DashboardStrings.home,
                index: 0,
              ),
              _buildNavItem(
                icon: Icons.history,
                label: DashboardStrings.history,
                index: 1,
              ),
              _buildNavItem(
                icon: Icons.person,
                label: DashboardStrings.profile,
                index: 2,
              ),
              _buildNavItem(
                icon: Icons.settings,
                label: DashboardStrings.settings,
                index: 3,
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildNavItem({
    required IconData icon,
    required String label,
    required int index,
  }) {
    final bool isActive = currentIndex == index;
    final Color color = isActive ? AppColors.primaryOrange : AppColors.grey;

    return InkWell(
      onTap: () => onTap(index),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 8),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Icon(
              icon,
              color: color,
              size: 24,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: TextStyle(
                color: color,
                fontSize: 11,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 161: custom_button.dart
**Path:** `lib\widgets\custom_button.dart`
**Size:** 2.34 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../constants/app_colors.dart';

class CustomButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final String text;
  final VoidCallback? onPressed;
  final Color? backgroundColor;
  final Color? textColor;
  final bool isLoading;
  final double? width;
  final double height;
  final double borderRadius;
  final bool hasShadow;

  const CustomButton({
    super.key,
    required this.text,
    this.onPressed,
    this.backgroundColor,
    this.textColor,
    this.isLoading = false,
    this.width,
    this.height = 56,
    this.borderRadius = 16,
    this.hasShadow = true,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final bool isDisabled = onPressed == null && !isLoading;
    final Color btnColor = backgroundColor ?? AppColors.primaryOrange;
    final Color btnTextColor = textColor ?? AppColors.white;

    return Container(
      width: width,
      height: height,
      decoration: hasShadow && !isDisabled
          ? BoxDecoration(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(borderRadius),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: btnColor.withOpacity(0.3),
            blurRadius: 20,
            offset: const Offset(0, 10),
          ),
        ],
      )
          : null,
      child: ElevatedButton(
        onPressed: isLoading ? null : onPressed,
        style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
          backgroundColor: isDisabled
              ? AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5)
              : btnColor,
          disabledBackgroundColor: AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5),
          shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(borderRadius),
          ),
          elevation: 0,
          padding: EdgeInsets.zero,
        ),
        child: isLoading
            ? SizedBox(
          height: 24,
          width: 24,
          child: CircularProgressIndicator(
            strokeWidth: 2.5,
            valueColor: AlwaysStoppedAnimation<Color>(btnTextColor),
          ),
        )
            : Text(
          text,
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 18,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            color: isDisabled ? AppColors.slateGrey.withOpacity(0.5) : btnTextColor,
            letterSpacing: 0.5,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../constants/dashboard_strings.dart';

class FilingForm extends StatefulWidget {
  final List<String> months;
  final List<String> years;
  final Function(String month, String year) onStartFiling;

  const FilingForm({
    super.key,
    required this.months,
    required this.years,
    required this.onStartFiling,
  });

  @override
  State<FilingForm> createState() => _FilingFormState();
}

class _FilingFormState extends State<FilingForm> {
  String? selectedMonth;
  String? selectedYear;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    // âœ… FIXED: Added null checks for both lists
    selectedMonth = widget.months.isNotEmpty ? widget.months.first : null;
    selectedYear = widget.years.isNotEmpty ? widget.years.first : null;
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    // âœ… FIXED: Handle empty lists
    if (widget.months.isEmpty || widget.years.isEmpty) {
      return Container(
        margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: AppColors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          border: Border.all(color: AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5)),
        ),
        child: const Center(
          child: Text(
            'No filing periods available',
            style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.grey),
          ),
        ),
      );
    }

    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        border: Border.all(color: AppColors.lightGrey.withOpacity(0.5)),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: AppColors.primaryBlue.withOpacity(0.05),
            blurRadius: 20,
            offset: const Offset(0, 4),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          _buildHeader(),
          const SizedBox(height: 20),
          _buildDropdowns(),
          const SizedBox(height: 20),
          _buildStartButton(),

    );

            color: AppColors.primaryBlue,
            fontSize: 16,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildDropdowns() {
    return Row(
      children: [
        // Month Dropdown
        Expanded(
          child: Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              const Text(
                DashboardStrings.monthLabel,
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: AppColors.grey,
                  fontSize: 11,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  letterSpacing: 0.5,
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(height: 8),
              Container(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12),
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  color: AppColors.backgroundGrey,
                  borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
                  border: Border.all(color: AppColors.lightGrey),
                ),
                child: DropdownButton<String>(
                  value: selectedMonth,
                  isExpanded: true,
                  underline: const SizedBox(),
                  icon: const Icon(Icons.keyboard_arrow_down,
                      color: AppColors.primaryOrange),
                  items: widget.months.map((month) {
                    return DropdownMenuItem<String>(
                      value: month,
                      child: Text(
                        month,
                        style: const TextStyle(
                          color: AppColors.primaryBlue,
                          fontSize: 14,
                          fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                        ),
                      ),
                    );
                  }).toList(),
                  onChanged: (value) {
                    setState(() => selectedMonth = value);
                  },
                  hint: const Text(DashboardStrings.selectMonth),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(width: 12),
        // Year Dropdown
        Expanded(
          child: Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              const Text(
                DashboardStrings.yearLabel,
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: AppColors.grey,
                  fontSize: 11,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  letterSpacing: 0.5,
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(height: 8),
              Container(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12),
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  color: AppColors.backgroundGrey,
                  borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
                  border: Border.all(color: AppColors.lightGrey),
                ),
                child: DropdownButton<String>(
                  value: selectedYear,
                  isExpanded: true,
                  underline: const SizedBox(),
                  icon: const Icon(Icons.keyboard_arrow_down,
                      color: AppColors.primaryOrange),
                  items: widget.years.map((year) {
```
